<br>\n\t\t\t\t\t}}\n\t\t\t\t\tThe '''Indian Institute of Technology, Rupnagar''' (currently functional) at [[IIT Delhi]], forms a part of the league along with 16 (7 existing, 9 proposed) other [[IIT]]s in [[India]].\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe seven old IITs are located in [[Indian Institute of Technology Kharagpur|Kharagpur]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Bombay|Bombay]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Madras|Madras]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Kanpur|Kanpur]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Delhi|Delhi]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Guwahati|Guwahati]], and [[Indian Institute of Technology Roorkee|Roorkee]]. With the plan to setup eight more IITs in the states of [[Rajasthan]], [[Bihar]] ([[Patna]]), [[Andhra Pradesh]] ([[Hyderabad, India| Hyderabad]]), [[Himachal Pradesh]], [[Orissa]] ([[Bhubaneshwar]]), [[Madhya Pradesh]] ([[Indore]]), [[Gujarat]] ([[Gandhinagar]]) and [[Punjab (India)|Punjab]] ([[Rupnagar]]), and the conversion of [[IT-BHU]] to an IIT, the total number of IITs will be increased to 16.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==History==\n\t\t\t\t\tThis new institute was established by MHRD, Govt.of India in year 2008. The proposed location for IIT-RN is Birla Farm, [[Rupnagar]], district headquarter of [[Punjab (India)|Punjab]] near to [[Chandigarh]]. The classes for current academic session are currently being held at [[IIT Delhi]].\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic Programs==\n\t\t\t\t\tIn its first year, i.e. academic year 2008-2009, three programmes will be offered. \n\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Computer Science and Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Electrical Engineering]] \n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Mechanical Engineering]] \n\n\t\t\t\t\tAdmission to these programmes is through the JEE and students are admitted after completing 10+2 schooling\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==External Delhi]].``\t\t==Location==`\t\tIIT of Punjab will be located at Roopnagar (formerly known as [[Ropar]]) town of the district Roopnagar. Roopnagar was founded in the 11th century and named after Rup Sen son of Raja Rokeshar. Recent excavations and explorations conducted at Roopnagar indicate that the first settlements here were the [[Harappan]]s, who reached the upper [[Satluj]] towards the close of third millenium B.C. The district has rich historical and religious significance. <br><br>Roopnagar town, the district headquarters is '42' km. from [[Chandigarh]], the state capital. Roopnagar is well connected by road on [[Indian National Highways|National Highway]] [[NH_21|NH^21]]. The [[Delhi]]^[[Ambala]]^[[Una]] railway line passes through Roopnagar and provides good [[rail]] connectivity. The nearest [[airport]] is at Chandigarh at a distance of about '60' km. Surrapa|\n\t\t\t\t\tundergrad      = 240|\n\t\t\t\t\tpostgrad       = 00|\n\t\t\t\t\tfree_label     = Acronym|iitrpr\n\t\t\t\t\tfree           = IIT RN|\n\t\t\t\t\tcity           = [[Rupnagar]] |\n\t\t\t\t\tstate          = [[Punjab (India)|Punjab]] |\n\t\t\t\t\tcountry        = [[India]] |\n\t\t\t\t\tcolors         =  |\n\t\t\t\t\tcampus         = 520 acres|\n\t\t\t\t\twebsite        = http://www.iitd.ac.in/iitrpr|\n\t\t\t\t\t}}\n\t\t\t\t\tThe '''Indian Institute of Technology Ropar''' (had its first year at [[IIT Delhi]] and currently functional at its transit campus in Ropar), forms a part of the league along with 15 (7 existing, 8 proposed) other [[Indian Institutes of Technology|IITs]] in [[India]].\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe seven old IITs are located in [[Indian Institute of Technology Kharagpur|Kharagpur]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Bombay|Bombay]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Madras|Madras]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Kanpur|Kanpur]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Delhi|Delhi]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Guwahati|Guwahati]], and [[Indian Institute of Technology Roorkee|Roorkee]]. With the plan to setup eight more IITs in the states of [[Rajasthan]], [[Bihar]] ([[Patna]]), [[Andhra Pradesh]] ([[Hyderabad, India|Hyderabad]]), [[Himachal Pradesh]] ([[Mandi]]), [[Orissa]] ([[Bhubaneshwar]]), [[Madhya Pradesh]] ([[Indore]]), [[Gujarat]] ([[Gandhinagar]]) and [[Punjab (India)|Punjab]] ([[Rupnagar]]), the total number of IITs will be increased to 15.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==History==\n\t\t\t\t\tThis new institute was established by [[Ministry of Human Resource Development (India)|Ministry of Human Resource Development (MHRD)]] of the [[Government of India]] in year 2008. The proposed location for IIT Punjab is Birla seed Farms, [[Rupnagar]], district headquarter of [[Punjab (India)|Punjab]] near to [[Chandigarh]]. The classes for academic session 2008-2009 were held at [[IIT Delhi]].\n\n\t\t\t\t\tFoundation stone of IIT Punjab was laid down on 24th feb, 2009 by former Union HRD Minister Mr. Arjun singh.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tSecond year onwards IIT Punjab students has been shifted to its temporary campus (a former women's polytechnic) which is provided by the govt. of punjab. Classes are being held in its temporary campus i.e former women's polytechnic Ropar till its own main campus gets ready. Renovation of temporary campus is going on at pace and IIT Delhi administration had promised to make the campus ready for second year students and coming freshers before the beginning of academic session 2009-2010. Second academic session of IIT Punjab started from 20th of august, 2009. Curriculum for rest of the semesters has been announced to students on the day of their registration.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Location==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar is located at Rupnagar (formerly known as [[Ropar]]) town of the district Roopnagar. Roopnagar was founded in the 11th century and named after Rup Sen son of Raja Rokeshar. Recent excavations and explorations conducted at Roopnagar indicate that the first settlements here were the [[Harappan]]s, who reached the upper [[Satluj]] towards the close of third millennium B.C. The district has rich historical and religious significance. \n\t\t\t\t\tRoopnagar town, the district headquarters is 42&nbsp;km. from [[Chandigarh]], the state capital. Roopnagar is well connected by road on [[Indian National Highways|National Highway]] [[NH-21]]. The [[Delhi]]-[[Ambala]]-[[Una, Himachal Pradesh|Una]] railway line passes through Roopnagar and provides good [[Rail transport|rail]] connectivity. The nearest [[airport]] is at Chandigarh at a distance of about 60&nbsp;km. The [[Satluj]] river passes close to Roopnagar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Director==\n\t\t\t\t\tDirector for IIT Punjab has been announced by the government of India and the confirmed director is Dr. M. K. Surrapa who was a professor in dept. of metallurgy in IISc Bangalore. He has joined IIT Ropar since the beginning of academic session 2009-2010 at Ropar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic Programs==\n\t\t\t\t\tIn its first year, i.e. academic year 2008-2009, three undergraduate programmes were offered. Admission to these programmes is through the JEE and students are admitted after completing 10+2 schooling.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Computer Science and Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Electrical Engineering]] \n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Mechanical Engineering]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar also invited admissions for K. Surrapa|\n\t\t\t\t\tundergrad      = 240|\n\t\t\t\t\tpostgrad       = 11|\n\t\t\t\t\tfree_label     = Acronym|iitrpr\n\t\t\t\t\tfree           = IIT RN|\n\t\t\t\t\tcity           = [[Rupnagar]] |\n\t\t\t\t\tstate          = [[Punjab (India)|Punjab]] |\n\t\t\t\t\tcountry        = [[India]] |\n\t\t\t\t\tcolors         =  |\n\t\t\t\t\tcampus         = 520 acres|\n\t\t\t\t\twebsite        = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in|\n\t\t\t\t\t}}\n\t\t\t\t\tThe '''Indian Institute of Technology Ropar''', or '''IIT Ropar''', sometimes also referred to as '''Indian Institute of Technology Punjab'''  ('''IIT Punjab''') is one of the 8 new [[Indian Institutes of Technology|IITs]] which have recently become functional.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe IITs are located in [[Indian Institute of Technology Kharagpur|Kharagpur]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Bombay|Bombay]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Madras|Madras]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Kanpur|Kanpur]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Delhi|Delhi]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Guwahati|Guwahati]], and [[Indian Institute of Technology Roorkee|Roorkee]], [[Rajasthan]],  [[Patna]], [[Hyderabad, India|Hyderabad]], [[Mandi]], [[Bhubaneshwar]], [[Indore]], [[Gandhinagar]] and [[Ropar]].\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==History==\n\t\t\t\t\tThis new institute was established by [[Ministry of Human Resource Development (India)|Ministry of Human Resource Development (MHRD)]] of the [[Government of India]] in year 2008. The proposed location for IIT Punjab is Birla seed Farms, Ropar ([[Rupnagar]]), district headquarter of [[Punjab (India)|Punjab]] near to [[Chandigarh]]. The classes for academic session 2008-2009 were held at [[IIT Delhi]]. The Institute is  now functional at its transit campus in Rupnagar. Foundation stone of IIT Punjab was laid down on 24th feb, 2009 by former Union HRD Minister [[Arjun Singh|Mr. Arjun Singh]].\n\n\t\t\t\t\tFrom the second year onwards, IIT Punjab students have been shifted to its temporary campus (a former women's polytechnic) provided by the govt. of punjab. Classes are being held in its temporary campus i.e former women's polytechnic Rupnagar till its own main campus gets ready. Renovation of temporary campus is going on steadily and IIT Delhi administration is making the campus ready for second year students and coming freshers before the beginning of academic session 2009-2010. Second academic session of IIT Punjab started from 20th of august, 2009. Curriculum for rest of the semesters has been announced to students on the day of their registration.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tGovt. of Punjab has already approved land for permanent campus of about 525 acres in Rupnagar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Location==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar is located at Rupnagar (formerly known as [[Ropar]]) town of the [[Rupnagar district|district Rupnagar]]. Rupnagar was founded in the 11th century and named after Rup Sen son of Raja Rokeshar. Recent excavations and explorations conducted at Rupnagar indicate that the first settlements here were the [[Harappan]]s, who reached the upper [[Satluj]] towards the close of third millennium B.C. The district has rich historical and religious significance. \n\n\t\t\t\t\tRupnagar town, the district headquarters is 42&nbsp;km. from [[Chandigarh]], the state capital. Rupnagar is well connected by road on [[Indian National Highways|National Highway]] [[NH-21]]. The [[Delhi]]-[[Ambala]]-[[Una, Himachal Pradesh|Una]] railway line passes through Rupnagar and provides good [[Rail transport|rail]] connectivity. The nearest [[airport]] is at Chandigarh at a distance of about 60&nbsp;km. The [[Satluj]] river passes close to Rupnagar. \n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe climate is charactrized by its general dryness, execpt during the south-west monsoon season, a hot summer and a cold winter. The winter is from mid-Neovember to February, summer from March to June and the monsoon from late June to mid-September. The average annual rainfall in the district is about 776&nbsp;mm with about 78% in the period of June to September.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe current temporary location is a brief 1.5km walk from Rupnagar railway station and the permanent campus is about 4-5 km from it.\n\t\t\t\t\t==Director==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe government of India has appointed Dr. M. K. Surrapa as director of IIT Ropar. He was a professor in dept. of metallurgy in [[IISc Bangalore|IISc Bangalore]]. He has joined IIT Ropar since the beginning of academic session 2009-2010 at Rupnagar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic Programs==\n\t\t\t\t\tIn its first year, i.e. academic year 2008-2009, three undergraduate programmes were offered. Admission to these programmes is through the JEE and students are admitted after completing 10+2 schooling.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Computer Science and Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Electrical Engineering]] \n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Mechanical Engineering]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Roparinvited admissions for Ph.D. in Mechancial Engg., Electrical Engg., [[Physics]], [[Chemistry]], [[Mathematics]] and [[Philosophy]] from 2009 session and was gifted with a high profile candidates for the same.<ref>http://www.iitd.ac.in/iitrpr/Admission.htm</ref>.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic Information==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute campus developed almost fully by the winter semester of academic session 2009-2010. The first half of academic year 2009-2010 was overseen by faculty from IIT Delhi.  IIT Ropar has also been in talks with three of  UK's best universities.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tUK institutes,with being quite impressed by the state of art facilities, have extended their support by signing MOU's in various direction.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe director of the institute, along with HRD minister Mr. Kapil Sibbal formally visited them in UK to share experiences, with their response reciprocated by an senior official from UK visiting the campus in the month of February.\n \n\t\t\t\t\tStudents from IInd year have been a great opportunity to explore themselves under the able guidance of collaborated UK universities in the months of May-June.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Collaborations in hand and the future plans==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar is keen to start collaborative ventures with university(both in India and abroad), industry, and other research institute. In sequel to the agreement signed between the Prime Minister of India and its counterpart in UK in JUne 2008, a number of universities and their consortia have expressed keen interest in collaborating with IIT Ropar. In the last few months, the Director, Prof. Surappa, has signed a number of MOUs with his counterparts in various universities in the United Kingdom. They have also had several visitors from universities abroad with a view to establish partnership in research and teaching.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe details are well elaborated at <ref>http://www.ukieri.org/Minister-Pat-McFadden-visit-Feb2010.htm</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus Life/Infrastructure==\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe campus is well equipped with two hostels for boys(each for Ist year and IInd year students) and one for the girls. The hostel area has all sorts of provision ranging from provisional store, barber shop, laundry all available at a quite reasonable rate.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe campus has been well credited with being the best campus in all new IIT's being independently administrated by the officials of IIT Punjab.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tCampus has well recruited manpower to cater the needs of the students.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tAll the hostels are well connected with a hi-speed wi-fi connection provided by BSNL and there are plans to expand the same.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Research or inspiration from the innovation==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute, apart from establishing robust teaching environment, is keen to facilitate and support cutting-edge research in a variety of areas. This aspect, we believe, will enable the students to acquaint themselves with latest development in their respective areas of study and pursue their own research interests. This would also result in a constant revision of the contents of courses that are being taught. \n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute encourages its faculty members to initiate research work and provides an initiation grant and also the basic facilities for its sustenance. It also encourages faculty members to establish collaborative research ventures with other research lab and industry. In this regard, the institute is keen to establish Central Research Facility. The institute has already started its PhD programme, so that the research environment is further augmented, expanded, and made even more vibrant.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Extra curriculum acts== \n\n\t\t\t\t\tWithin the campus, there are adequate and excellent  playgrounds for major sports as cricket, basketball, tennis, football with a qualified coach in each department.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tIndoor games include chess, table tennis, carom,etc., as constituents of the SAC.  =  |\n\t\t\t\t\tname           = Indian Institute of Technology <br> Ropar  |\n\t\t\t\t\tlogo           = [[Image:Logo IIT Ropar.jpg|center|100px|IIT Ropar Logo]]|\n\t\t\t\t\ttype           = [[Education]] and [[Research]] [[Institution]] |\n\t\t\t\t\testablished    = 2008 |\n\t\t\t\t\tdirector       = Dr. M. K. Surrapa|\n\t\t\t\t\tundergrad      = 360|\n\t\t\t\t\tpostgrad       = 22|\n\t\t\t\t\tfree_label     = Acronym|iitrpr\n\t\t\t\t\tfree           = IIT RN|\n\t\t\t\t\tcity           = [[Rupnagar]] |\n\t\t\t\t\tstate          = [[Punjab (India)|Punjab]] |\n\t\t\t\t\tcountry        = [[India]] |\n\t\t\t\t\tcolors         =  |\n\t\t\t\t\tcampus         = Urban, Spread over {{convert|520|acre|km2}}|\n\t\t\t\t\twebsite        = [http://www.iitrpr.ac.in|http://www.iitrprstudents.com] |\n\n\t\t\t\t\t}}\n\t\t\t\t\tThe '''Indian Institute of Technology Ropar''', or '''IIT Ropar''',({{lang-hi|\u092d\u093e\u0930\u0924\u0940\u092f \u092a\u094d\u0930\u094c\u0926\u094d\u092f\u094b\u0917\u093f\u0915\u0940 \u0938\u0902\u0938\u094d\u0925\u093e\u0928 \u0930\u094b\u092a\u0921\u093c}}) sometimes also referred to as '''Indian Institute of Technology Punjab'''  ('''IIT Punjab''') is one of the 8 new [[Indian Institutes of Technology|IITs]] which have recently become functional.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe IITs are located in [[Indian Institute of Technology Kharagpur|Kharagpur]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Bombay|Bombay]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Madras|Madras]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Kanpur|Kanpur]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Delhi|Delhi]], [[Indian Institute of Technology Guwahati|Guwahati]], and [[Indian Institute of Technology Roorkee|Roorkee]], [[Rajasthan]],  [[Patna]], [[Hyderabad, India|Hyderabad]], [[Mandi, Himachal Pradesh, India|Mandi]], [[Bhubaneshwar]], [[Indore]], [[Gandhinagar]] and [[Ropar]].\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==History==\n\t\t\t\t\tThis new institute was established by [[Ministry of Human Resource Development (India)|Ministry of Human Resource Development (MHRD)]] of the [[Government of India]] in year 2008. The proposed location for IIT Punjab is Birla seed Farms, Ropar ([[Rupnagar]]), district headquarter of [[Punjab (India)|Punjab]] near to [[Chandigarh]]. The classes for academic session 2008-2009 were held at [[IIT Delhi]]. The Institute is  now functional at its transit campus in Rupnagar. Foundation stone of IIT Punjab was laid down on 24th feb, 2009 by former Union HRD Minister [[Arjun Singh|Mr. Arjun Singh]].\n\n\t\t\t\t\tFrom the second year onwards, IIT Punjab students have been shifted to its temporary campus (a former women's polytechnic) provided by the government of Punjab. Classes are being held in its temporary campus i.e, former women's polytechnic Rupnagar till its own main campus gets ready. Renovation of temporary campus is going on steadily and IIT Delhi administration is making the campus ready for second year students and coming freshers before the beginning of academic session 2009-2010. Second academic session of IIT Punjab started from 20th of august, 2009. Curriculum for rest of the semesters has been announced to students on the day of their registration.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe government of Punjab has already approved land for permanent campus of about 525 acres in Rupnagar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Location==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar is located at Rupnagar (formerly known as [[Ropar]]) town of the [[Rupnagar district|district Rupnagar]]. Rupnagar was founded in the 11th century and named after Rup Sen son of Raja Rokeshar. Recent excavations and explorations conducted at Rupnagar indicate that the first settlements here were the [[Harappan]]s, who reached the upper [[Satluj]] towards the close of third millennium B.C. The district has rich historical and religious significance.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tRupnagar town, the district headquarters is 42&nbsp;km. from [[Chandigarh]], the state capital. Rupnagar is well connected by road on [[Indian National Highways|National Highway]] [[NH-21]]. The [[Delhi]]-[[Ambala]]-[[Una, Himachal Pradesh|Una]] railway line passes through Rupnagar and provides good [[Rail transport|rail]] connectivity. The nearest [[airport]] is at Chandigarh at a distance of about 60&nbsp;km. The [[Satluj]] river passes close to Rupnagar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe climate is characterized by its general dryness, except during the south-west monsoon season, a hot summer and a cold winter. The winter is from mid-November to February, summer from March to June and the monsoon from late June to mid-September. The average annual rainfall in the district is about 776&nbsp;mm with about 78% in the period of June to September.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe current temporary location is a brief 1.5&nbsp;km walk from Rupnagar railway station and the permanent campus is about 4\u20135&nbsp;km from it.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic system==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe curriculum followed at IIT Ropar provides for a science-based engineering education, with a view to produce quality engineer-scientists. If facilitates broad-based knowledge acquisition and, simultaneously, nurtures a temper for life-long learning and exploration. Students are encouraged to go beyond the classroom to conduct and carry out independent work by means of research projects, guided reading, and by allowing them to join the research activities undertaken by faculty members. The idea behind such a fashioning of the curriculum is the belief that classroom activities must be supplemented by independent study and also by individual research that broadens one's horizon and provides for opportunities to bring one's ideas to fruition.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe academic programme at the institute follows a semester-based credit system. The prominent feature of the credit system is the process of continuous evaluation of a student's performance and the flexibility to allow a student to progress at an an optimum pace suited to his/her ability or convenience, subject to fulfilling minimum requirements for continuation. A minimum Grade Point Average (GPA) is necessary for satisfactory progress and continuation in the programme. \n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic programmes==\n\t\t\t\t\tIn its first year, i.e. academic year 2008-2009, three undergraduate programmes were offered. Admission to these programmes is through the JEE and students are admitted after completing 10+2 schooling.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Computer Science and Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Electrical Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Mechanical Engineering]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\tA recent JEE rankings survey of new and existing IITs placed IIT Ropar on the top among new IITs <ref>http://www.inspirenignite.com/iit-ranking-2010/</ref>. The institute could find success recruiting in the U.S <ref>http://chronicle.com/article/An-Indian-University-Finds/123888/</ref>. IIT Ropar also offered admissions for Ph.D. in Mechanical Engineering, Electrical Engineering, [[Physics]], [[Chemistry]], [[Mathematics]] and [[Philosophy]] from 2009 session <ref>http://www.iitd.ac.in/iitrpr/Admission.htm</ref>.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic information==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute campus developed almost fully by the winter semester of academic session 2009-2010. The first half of academic year 2009-2010 was overseen by faculty from IIT Delhi.  IIT Ropar has also been in talks with three of  UK's best universities.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tUK institutes,with being quite impressed by the state of art facilities, have extended their support by signing MOU's in various direction.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe director of the institute, along with HRD minister Mr. Kapil Sibbal formally visited them in UK to share experiences, with their response reciprocated by a senior official from UK visiting the campus in the month of February.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tStudents from IInd year have been a great opportunity to explore themselves under the able guidance of collaborated UK universities in the months of May-June.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Collaborations in hand and the future plans==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar is keen to start collaborative ventures with university(both in India and abroad), industry, and other research institute. In sequel to the agreement signed between the Prime Minister of India and its counterpart in UK in June 2008, a number of universities and their consortia have expressed keen interest in collaborating with IIT Ropar. In the last few months, the Director, Prof. Surappa, has signed a number of MOUs with his counterparts in various universities in the United Kingdom. They have also had several visitors from universities abroad with a view to establish partnership in research and teaching.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe details are well elaborated at <ref>http://www.ukieri.org/Minister-Pat-McFadden-visit-Feb2010.htm</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus life/infrastructure==\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe campus is well equipped with three hostels for boys and one for the girls.One more hostel is being built for the 2011-12 batch of students. The hostel area has all sorts of provision ranging from provisional store, barber shop, laundry all available at a quite reasonable rate.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tInstitute has its own independent post office opened for the facilities of staffs and students of the institute.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tSBI(State Bank of India) has a well operational branch inside the campus premises, with talks of ATM being introduced in near early future.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe campus has been well credited with being the best campus in all new IIT's being independently administrated by the officials of IIT Ropar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tCampus has well recruited manpower to cater the needs of the students.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tAll the hostels are well connected with a hi-speed wi-fi and LAN connection provided by BSNL and there are plans to expand the same.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe beautiful campus has a peaceful environment.<ref>http://picasaweb.google.com/117707137521513270028</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Research or inspiration from the innovation==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute, apart from establishing robust teaching environment, is keen to facilitate and support cutting-edge research in a variety of areas. This aspect, we believe, will enable the students to acquaint themselves with latest development in their respective areas of study and pursue their own research interests. This would also result in a constant revision of the contents of courses that are being taught.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute encourages its faculty members to initiate research work and provides an initiation grant and also the basic facilities for its sustenance. It also encourages faculty members to establish collaborative research ventures with other research lab and industry. In this regard, the institute is keen to establish Central Research Facility. The institute has already started its PhD programme, so that the research environment is further augmented, expanded, and made even more vibrant.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Extra curriculum acts==\n\n\t\t\t\t\tWithin the campus, there are adequate and excellent  playgrounds for major sports as cricket, basketball, tennis, football with a qualified coach in each department.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tIndoor games include chess, table tennis, carom,etc., as constituents of the SAC. Other SAC utilities include various musical instruments such as drum, guitar(Electric and Acoustic) and piano, with an extra provision for the electronic ones.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Clubs===\n\t\t\t\t\tThere are various clubs being run at the institute like Chess, Athletic, Creative Writing, Science and Technology, etc. managed by the respective representatives  and a secretary to guide them.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Creative writing===\n\t\t\t\t\tTo develop the creative side of a students' mind, inputs given by students are being published at regular intervals with articles ranging from various fields.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Inter-IIT sports meet===\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar participated in the inter IIT sports meet held at IIT Kanpur. IIT Ropar performed quiet brilliantly in various sports and won medals in many of them.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Mess facilities===\n\t\t\t\t\tMess has provision to all the cuisines in India. The hostels 1 -1 well equipped for comfortable lodging 1 boarding of approximately '380' students. All hostels are provided with water coolers and RO systems. Each hostel has a common room that provides facilities for indoor recreation and games. The hostel complex also includes four shops that cater to the basic needs of the residents, and also a few washing machine facility. High speed internet is available via wi^fi and LAN connections provided by BSNL.`\t\tThe day^to^day management of hostels is taken care of by a committee consisting of student representatives. Each hostel has a warden, who guides the students to manage the affairs of the hostels.`\t\tInstitute has its own independent post office opened for the facilities of staffs and students of the institute. SBI (State Bank of India) has a well operational branch inside the campus premises, with talks of ATM being introduced in near early future.``\t\t===Medical Facility===`\t\tThe institute has allocated a separate building, which adjoins the hostel complex, for its medical facility. The bill for the addition of these eight IITs and the conversion of [[Institute of Technology, Banaras Hindu University]] to IIT<ref name=AmendmentAct>{{cite web|url=http://www.prsindia.org/uploads/media/Institute%20of%20Technology%20Bill%202010.pdf|format=PDF|title=The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Bill, 2010}}</ref> was passed in the [[Lok Sabha]] in March 24, 2011<ref>{{cite web |url= http://www.deccanherald.com/content/148456/ls-passes-bill-provide-iit.html |title=LS passes bill to provide IIT status to 8 institutes, BHU  |work=deccanherald.com |date=March 24, 2011 |accessdate=9 May 2011}}</ref> and is still to be adopted by the [[Rajya Sabha]].\n\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar was set up by the [[Ministry of Human Resource Development (India)|Ministry of Human Resource Development]] (MHRD), [[Government of India]], to expand the reach and enhance the quality of technical education in the country. This institute is committed to providing state-of-the-art technical education in a variety of fields and also for facilitating transmission of knowledge in keeping with latest developments in pedagogy. These two areas of focus will enable students to gain exposure to recent trends in their chosen domains of study and gain practical experience through a wide variety of activities the institute facilitates in its own campus and arranges for in collaboration with industry and other institutes.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==History==\n\t\t\t\t\tThis new institute was established by MHRD in year 2008. The classes for academic session 2008-2009 were held at [[IIT Delhi]]. The Institute started functioning from its transit campus in Rupnagar in August 2009.<ref>http://twocircles.net/2009aug07/iit_punjab_start_working_its_new_campus_aug_20.html</ref><ref>http://articles.timesofindia.indiatimes.com/2009-07-21/india/28211741_1_transit-campus-ropar-iit-delhi</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus & Location==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar is located at Rupnagar (formerly known as [[Ropar]]) town of the [[Rupnagar district|district Rupnagar]]. Rupnagar was founded in the 11th century and named after Rup Sen son of Raja Rokeshar. Recent excavations and explorations conducted at Rupnagar indicate that the first settlements here were the [[Harappan]]s, who reached the upper [[Satluj]] towards the close of third millennium B.C. The district has rich historical and religious significance.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tRupnagar town, the district headquarters is 42 km. from [[Chandigarh]], the state capital. Rupnagar is well connected by road on [[Indian National Highways|National Highway]] [[NH-21]]. The [[Delhi]]-[[Ambala]]-[[Una, Himachal Pradesh|Una]] railway line passes through Rupnagar and provides good [[Rail transport|rail]] connectivity. The nearest [[airport]] is at Chandigarh at a distance of about 60 km. The [[Satluj]] river passes close to Rupnagar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe climate is characterized by its general dryness, except during the south-west monsoon season, a hot summer and a cold winter. The winter is from mid-November to February, summer from March to June and the monsoon from late June to mid-September. The average annual rainfall in the district is about 776 mm with about 78% in the period of June to September.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Permanent Campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe location for permanent campus of IIT Ropar is Birla Seed Farms, Ropar ([[Rupnagar]]), district headquarter of Ropar ([[Rupnagar]]) near to [[Chandigarh]]. The Institute is expected to be operational from its permanent campus by 2013. The Government of Punjab has already approved land for permanent campus of about {{convert|525|acre|km2}} in Rupnagar. Foundation stone for permanent campus of IIT Ropar was laid down on 24 February 2009 by former Union HRD Minister [[Arjun Singh|Mr. Arjun Singh]].\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Temporary Campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe temporary campus of IIT Ropar is former Women's Polytechnic, Rupnagar. The academic and administration buildings have been completely renovated to accommodate all the requirements of the Institute . It has all the basic infrastructure to run Academic programmes specially designed by IIT Delhi. The transit campus is equipped with state of art lecture halls along with well maintained playgrounds to nurture the bright minds and enhance their overall development. Special emphasis has been laid to set up advanced laboratories to help students gain practical insight of the courses that are a part of their curriculum.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe current temporary campus is a brief 1 km walk from Rupnagar railway station and the permanent campus is about 4\u20135 km from it.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic system==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe curriculum followed at IIT Ropar provides for a science-based engineering education, with a view to produce quality engineer-scientists. If facilitates broad-based knowledge acquisition and, simultaneously, nurtures a temper for life-long learning and exploration. Students are encouraged to go beyond the classroom to conduct and carry out independent work by means of research projects, guided reading, and by allowing them to join the research activities undertaken by faculty members. The idea behind such a fashioning of the curriculum is the belief that classroom activities must be supplemented by independent study and also by individual research that broadens one's horizon and provides for opportunities to bring one's ideas to fruition.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe academic programme at the institute follows a semester-based credit system. The prominent feature of the credit system is the process of continuous evaluation of a student's performance and the flexibility to allow a student to progress at an an optimum pace suited to his/her ability or convenience, subject to fulfilling minimum requirements for continuation. A minimum Grade Point Average (GPA) is necessary for satisfactory progress and continuation in the programme.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic programmes==\n\t\t\t\t\tIn its first year, i.e. academic year 2008-2009, three undergraduate programmes were offered. Admission to these programmes is through the JEE and students are admitted after completing 10+2 (high-school level) schooling.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Computer Science and Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Electrical Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Mechanical Engineering]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar also offers admissions for Ph.D. in Computer Science and Engineering, Mechanical Engineering, Electrical Engineering, [[Physics]], [[Chemistry]], [[Mathematics]] and [[Philosophy]].<ref>http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic information==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute's transit campus developed almost fully by the winter semester of academic session 2009-2010. The first half of academic year 2009-2010 was overseen by faculty from IIT Delhi.  IIT Ropar has also been in talks with three of the United Kingdom's best universities.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe UK institutes, with being quite impressed by the state of art facilities at IIT Ropar, have extended their support by signing MoU's in various directions.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Director of the institute, Prof. M.K. Surappa, along with HRD minister Mr. Kapil Sibbal formally visited the universities in UK to share experiences, with their response reciprocated by a senior official from UK visiting the campus in the month of February.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tStudents of the 2008 batch have had a great opportunity to explore their academic abilities under the able guidance of collaborated UK universities in the months of May\u2013June, 2010.<ref>http://www1.aston.ac.uk/international-students/international-news/news-archive/july-2010/aston-university-welcomes-iit-ropar-students/</ref>\n\t\t\t\t\tThe students of the 2008 batch are currently (for the summer period of 2011, May-July) undergoing Industrial Training & Research at various leading industries, companies and other research institutes (such as Microsoft, Bell Labs, Aston University-UK, CSIO-India, Bharti Airtel, Hero Honda, Maruti Suzuki, etc.) in their respective fields. The 2009 batch, now moving to their third academic year (2011-2012) are pursuing their interests through research programmes in various institutes (including Aston University, UK) for the same summer period.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Collaborations in hand and the future plans==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar is keen to start collaborative ventures with universities, industries, and other research institutes (both in India and outside India). In sequel to the agreement signed between the Prime Minister of India and its counterpart in UK in June 2008, a number of universities and their consortia have expressed keen interest in collaborating with IIT Ropar. In the last few months, the Director, Prof. Surappa, has signed a number of MOUs with his counterparts in various universities in the United Kingdom. They have also had several visitors from universities abroad with a view to establish partnership in research and teaching.<ref>http://www.indianexpress.com/news/uk-tieup-on-cards-for-iiserpune-iitpunja/559079/</ref><ref>http://www.ukieri.org/Minister-Pat-McFadden-visit-Feb2010.htm</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Research or inspiration from the innovation==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute, apart from establishing robust teaching environment, is keen to facilitate and support cutting-edge research in a variety of areas. This aspect will enable the students to acquaint themselves with latest development in their respective areas of study and pursue their own research interests. This would also result in a constant revision of the contents of courses that are being taught.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute encourages its faculty members to initiate research work and provides an initiation grant and also the basic facilities for its sustenance. It also encourages faculty members to establish collaborative research ventures with other research lab and industry. In this regard, the institute is keen to establish Central Research Facility. The institute has already started its PhD programme, so that the research environment is further augmented, expanded, and made even more vibrant.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus life/Infrastructure==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Hostel Facilities===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Institute campus houses four hostels: three for boys and one for girls. The hostels are well equipped for comfortable lodging and boarding of approximately 380 students. All hostels are provided with water coolers and RO systems. Each hostel has a common room that provides facilities for indoor recreation and games. The hostel complex also includes four shops that cater to the basic needs of the residents, and also a few washing machine facility. High speed internet is available via wireless internet (spread in the complete campus area) and LAN connections provided by BSNL.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe day-to-day management of hostels is taken care of by a committee consisting of student representatives, faculty members and administrative staff. Each hostel has a warden, who guides the students to manage the affairs of the hostels.\n\t\t\t\t\tInstitute has its own independent post office opened for the staff and students of the institute. SBI (State Bank of India) has a well operational branch inside the campus premises, with talks of ATM being introduced in near early future.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Medical Facility===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute has allocated a separate building, which adjoins the hostel complex, for its medical facility. A doctor and a nurse have been appointed to attend to medical emergencies of the campus residents. In addition the institute relies upon a few super-speciality hospitals in the city of Ropar for providing medical care to its members.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Sports Facilities===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe currently enrollled three batches (2008 entry, 2009 entry and 2010 entry) of students are, apart from showing excellent academic progress, keen to pursue their interests in sports and games. To nurture these interests, the institute has several facilities. At present, the institute has cricket field, three tennis courts, a football field, a hockey field, a gymnasium, a basket ball court and also a number of facilities for several athletic events. The institute also encourages its students to participate in inter-IIT sport events and other competitions. The appointment of a coach has further augmented sports-related activities in the campus.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Students Activity Centre(SAC) has a well equipped gymnasium and supports a music room, available for the students.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Central Library===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Central Library functions as the primary information resource and repository for all teaching and research activities at the institute. Apart from textbooks and recommended reading material prescribed for each course offered at the institute, the library houses a growing collection of research monographs, reports, multi-volume reference works, dictionaries, encyclopedias, handbooks, and so on. In addition, the library also facilitates access to a number of journals through its participation in consortia such as INDEST-AICTE. At present, users can consult more than 4000 books (available on shelves) and hundreds of journals (through electronic subscription).<ref>http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/centrallibrary.shtml</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Security===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute has ensured that its campus and residents are safe and secure. To accomplish this, a security agency has been entrusted with the task of providing security to its personnel and resources.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe beautiful campus has a peaceful environment.<ref>http://picasaweb.google.com/117707137521513270028</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Extra Curricular Activities==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Societies & Clubs===\n\t\t\t\t\tThere are various societies being run by the student body at the institute to promote extra currulicular and co-curricular activities. These clubs ensure participation from the students in different institute level activities & competitions, and prepare them for inter-college competitions. The Music Society, The Dance Club, LitSoc- The Literary Society, The Chess Club, The Athletics Club, The Creative Writing Club, Science and Technology Club, etc. are managed by the respective student representatives and a secretary.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Zeitgeist===\n\t\t\t\t\tZeitgeist is the annual cultural fest of IIT Ropar. It is typically held in autumn(Sept/Oct) and aims at being one of the biggest student festival in Punjab. It took birth in the year 2010, when students of the institution came together to organise the event in September. The theme for the first edition of the festival was 'The Spirit of the Times' (the meaning of Zeitgeist) and the fest attracted participation from colleges in far-off places such as Delhi, Roorkee, Mandi and from many places in Punjab and Haryana. The title sponsors for the event were Hero Honda and the star performers were Faridkot, The Band. The fest encouraged spread of Indian culture through its events, with a Spic Macay event being a part of the inaugural ceremony. The student body at IIT Ropar aims to bring back the festive mood to Punjab and the adjoining states in the coming September, 2011.\n\t\t\t\t\t<ref>http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/city/chandigarh/Ropar-IIT-gets-its-cultural-icon/articleshow/6674627.cms</ref>\n\t\t\t\t\t<ref>http://www.zeitgeistfest.com</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==See also==\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[List of universities in India]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[Indian Institutes of Technology]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[Education in India]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==References==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Reflist}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==External links==\n\t\t\t\t\t*[http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/ IIT Ropar (Punjab) official site]\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Indian Institute Of Technology}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t{{DEFAULTSORT:Indian Institute Of Technology Punjab}}\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Indian Institutes of Technology]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Technical universities and colleges]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Educational institutions established in 2008]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Rupnagar]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Education in Punjab (India)]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t[[no:Indian Institute of Technology Punjab]]\n\t\t\t\t"}, {"text": "795 it.`\t\t[[Image:http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/slideshow/5.jpg -1 ]]``\t\t==Academic 1450 "}, {"text": "795 -2 it.``\t\t==Academic 1450 "}, {"text": "1501 -1 vibrant.`\t\t== Entrepreneurship Cell ==`\t\t==== Funding opportunities for Prototype Development ====`\t\tWith the goal to foster innovation within industry, academia and government bodies in the state of Punjab IIT Ropar has launched a prototype development and innovation fund (PDIF). The PDIF has been established to address the technology gap between research labs and commercial products. The PDIF will fund projects that would validate the commercial potential of a technology and projects that serve the immediate technological needs of the nation in general and the regional industry in particular.``\t\t==Campus 744 "}, {"text": "1504 -7 ==`\t\tWith 75 -1 particular.`\t\tTypical project would be a partnership between the industry and the academia with a strong case for commercialization of the technology based on the prototype to be developed in the project. ``\t\t==Campus 744 "}, {"text": "1502 Rural Technology Action Group (RuTAG) ==`\t\tThe IIT^Ropar is the first among the new IITs in the country with a Rural Technology Action Group (RuTAG) Center on its campus. According to professor S V Raghavan, chairman, technical advisory committee, NKN, \u201cto begin with 1,200 major institutions including the IITs, CSIR laboratories, space research and atomic energy institutions will be connected digitally. The infrastructure bandwidth will facilitate high speed classroom sessions. You can even transmit satellite television programmes using the facility. With just '4' megabit connectivity an institution can simultaneously conduct up to '250' classroom sessions.\u201d``\t\tThe seamless integration provided by the high capacity NKN digital connectivity will help the academic and research community to establish countrywide classrooms, multicasting, streaming, video and voice conferencing, grid computing, digital libraries and collaboration portals. A professor from the IIT may not have the time to visit a rural college to deliver a guest lecture. Also not every institution may have the financial resources to arrange for guest faculty visits from premier research organisations.``\t\tInterestingly, this revolutionary bandwidth connectivity has been put in place by using the extensive Optical Fibre Cable (OFC) networks of the BSNL, Railtel and Power Grid Corporation of India Limited (PGCIL). In fact, Raghavan describes the underground OFC network as \u201cthe buried treasure of the nation\u201d which has now come in handy to create \u201can exciting win^win situation\u201d through a co^ownership pattern where the network operators stand to gain by selling additional bandwidth, while it facilitates knowledge sharing for educational institutions. The NKN was a joint initiative of the National Knowledge Commission and the union government. This network has the capacity to connect as many as 30,000 to 40,000 universities and colleges. `\t\t<ref>http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/nkn/</ref>``\t\t===Security===`\t\tThe 310 "}, {"text": "1029 -1 in^`\t\t1) 3 -1 Engineering,`\t\t2) 1 -1 Engineering,`\t\t3) 1 -1 Engineering,`\t\t4) -1 Physics `\t\t5) -1 Chemistry `\t\t6) -1 Mathematics -1 `\t\t7) -1 Philosophy.`\t\t<ref>http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml</ref>``\t\t==Academic 1886 "}, {"text": "1029 -1 in^`\t\t* 3 -1 Engineering,`\t\t* 1 -1 Engineering,`\t\t* 1 -1 Engineering,`\t\t* 1 -1 `\t\t* 1 -1 `\t\t* 1 -1 `\t\t* 1887 "}, {"text": "2336 -1 subscription).<ref>http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/centrallibrary.shtml</ref>`\t\t===NKN@IIT ROPAR^\"National -3 1 -1 Network\"===`\t\tThe 589 "}, {"text": "2829 was Hero Honda,Joint sponsor was BSNL,Associate sponsor 1 -2 ACC,ICON,Godrej intero,TIME 1 several other sponsors such as GAIL(India)limited,Design Tech,Desein,NTPC,Allahabad bank and many more..`\t\t 96 "}, {"text": "2850 more.the -2 95 "}, {"text": "677 -1 Campus===`\t\t[[File:Iit_ropar_campus.jpg|right|370px|IIT Ropar temporary campus ]]`\t\tThe 42 -1 Delhi.The -1 2224 "}, {"text": "677 -1 Campus===`\t\t[[File:Iit_ropar_campus.jpg|thumb|right|370px|IIT 2271 "}, {"text": "1227 -1 Suzuki,Nokia and Siemens 1721 "}, {"text": "2341 -1 subscription).<ref>http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/centrallibrary.shtml</ref>`\t\t===Security===`\t\tThe -282 327 "}, {"text": "677 Campus===`\t\tThe -5 42 -1 Delhi. RuTAG is conceptualized, initiated and sponsored by Principal Scientific Adviser Dr R Chidambaram, Government of India, to encourage rural technologies.``\t\tDr Chidambaram will inaugurate RuTAG on May 3. Such centers have been running in the older IITs. Officials say that RuTAG will help develop a network of government agencies and NGOs that will aid in research and development intervention in the rural sector.``\t\tThe aim of RuTAG is to upgrade rural systems to effective levels for boosting rural economy,new problem areas in the rural sector and provide research and development intervention whenever necessary.``\t\tAlso, the study of nuclear astrophysics is bound to get a momentum with the setting up of a nuclear physics instrumentation lab at the institute. This lab would help in radiation detection and high^spin isomeric state studies. It is working on a project which envisages producing power from bio fuel. The project is so modeled as to help at least three households produce their own power from bio fuel. The first prototype plant utilizing agri^waste to produce energy shall be inaugurated in early September.`\t\t<ref>http://www.4jat.com/jat_community_article.asp?jat_community=2708&subcat=Education</ref>``\t\t==Campus 744 "}, {"text": "1363 -1 teaching.<ref>http://www.indianexpress.com/news/uk^tieup^on^cards^for^iiserpune^iitpunja/559079/</ref><ref>http://www.ukieri.org/Minister^Pat^McFadden^visit^Feb2010.htm</ref>`\t\tThe IIT Ropar is the only new institute to have inked a letter of intent with Simon Fraser University. The bill for the addition of these eight IITs and the conversion of [[Institute of Technology, Banaras Hindu University]] to IIT<ref name=AmendmentAct>{{cite web|url=http://www.prsindia.org/uploads/media/Institute%20of%20Technology%20Bill%202010.pdf|format=PDF|title=The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Bill, 2010}}</ref> was passed in the [[Lok Sabha]] in March 24, 2011<ref>{{cite web |url= http://www.deccanherald.com/content/148456/ls-passes-bill-provide-iit.html |title=LS passes bill to provide IIT status to 8 institutes, BHU  |work=deccanherald.com |date=March 24, 2011 |accessdate=9 May 2011}}</ref> and is still to be adopted by the [[Rajya Sabha]].\n\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar was set up by the [[Ministry of Human Resource Development (India)|Ministry of Human Resource Development]] (MHRD), [[Government of India]], to expand the reach and enhance the quality of technical education in the country. This institute is committed to providing state-of-the-art technical education in a variety of fields and also for facilitating transmission of knowledge in keeping with latest developments in pedagogy. These two areas of focus will enable students to gain exposure to recent trends in their chosen domains of study and gain practical experience through a wide variety of activities the institute facilitates in its own campus and arranges for in collaboration with industry and other institutes.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==History==\n\t\t\t\t\tThis new institute was established by MHRD in year 2008. The classes for academic session 2008-2009 were held at [[IIT Delhi]]. The Institute started functioning from its transit campus in Rupnagar in August 2009.<ref>http://twocircles.net/2009aug07/iit_punjab_start_working_its_new_campus_aug_20.html</ref><ref>http://articles.timesofindia.indiatimes.com/2009-07-21/india/28211741_1_transit-campus-ropar-iit-delhi</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus & Location==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar is located at Rupnagar (formerly known as [[Ropar]]) town of the [[Rupnagar district|district Rupnagar]]. Rupnagar was founded in the 11th century and named after Rup Sen son of Raja Rokeshar. Recent excavations and explorations conducted at Rupnagar indicate that the first settlements here were the [[Harappan]]s, who reached the upper [[Satluj]] towards the close of third millennium B.C. The district has rich historical and religious significance.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tRupnagar town, the district headquarters is 42 km. from [[Chandigarh]], the state capital. Rupnagar is well connected by road on [[Indian National Highways|National Highway]] [[NH-21]]. The [[Delhi]]-[[Ambala]]-[[Una, Himachal Pradesh|Una]] railway line passes through Rupnagar and provides good [[Rail transport|rail]] connectivity. The nearest [[airport]] is at Chandigarh at a distance of about 60 km. The [[Satluj]] river passes close to Rupnagar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe climate is characterized by its general dryness, except during the south-west monsoon season, a hot summer and a cold winter. The winter is from mid-November to February, summer from March to June and the monsoon from late June to mid-September. The average annual rainfall in the district is about 776 mm with about 78% in the period of June to September.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Permanent Campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe location for permanent campus of IIT Ropar is Birla Seed Farms, Ropar ([[Rupnagar]]), district headquarter of Ropar ([[Rupnagar]]) near to [[Chandigarh]]. The Institute is expected to be operational from its permanent campus by 2013. The Government of Punjab has already approved land for permanent campus of about {{convert|525|acre|km2}} in Rupnagar. Foundation stone for permanent campus of IIT Ropar was laid down on 24 February 2009 by former Union HRD Minister [[Arjun Singh|Mr. Arjun Singh]].\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Temporary Campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe temporary campus of IIT Ropar is former Women's Polytechnic, Rupnagar. The academic and administration buildings have been completely renovated to accommodate all the requirements of the Institute . It has all the basic infrastructure to run Academic programmes specially designed by IIT Delhi. The transit campus is equipped with state of art lecture halls along with well maintained playgrounds to nurture the bright minds and enhance their overall development. Special emphasis has been laid to set up advanced laboratories to help students gain practical insight of the courses that are a part of their curriculum.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe current temporary campus is a brief 1 km walk from Rupnagar railway station and the permanent campus is about 4\u20135 km from it.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic system==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe curriculum followed at IIT Ropar provides for a science-based engineering education, with a view to produce quality engineer-scientists. If facilitates broad-based knowledge acquisition and, simultaneously, nurtures a temper for life-long learning and exploration. Students are encouraged to go beyond the classroom to conduct and carry out independent work by means of research projects, guided reading, and by allowing them to join the research activities undertaken by faculty members. The idea behind such a fashioning of the curriculum is the belief that classroom activities must be supplemented by independent study and also by individual research that broadens one's horizon and provides for opportunities to bring one's ideas to fruition.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe academic programme at the institute follows a semester-based credit system. The prominent feature of the credit system is the process of continuous evaluation of a student's performance and the flexibility to allow a student to progress at an an optimum pace suited to his/her ability or convenience, subject to fulfilling minimum requirements for continuation. A minimum Grade Point Average (GPA) is necessary for satisfactory progress and continuation in the programme.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic programmes==\n\t\t\t\t\tIn its first year, i.e. academic year 2008-2009, three undergraduate programmes were offered. Admission to these programmes is through the JEE and students are admitted after completing 10+2 (high-school level) schooling.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Computer Science and Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Electrical Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Mechanical Engineering]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar also offers admissions for Ph.D. in Computer Science and Engineering, Mechanical Engineering, Electrical Engineering, [[Physics]], [[Chemistry]], [[Mathematics]] and [[Philosophy]].<ref>http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic information==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute's transit campus developed almost fully by the winter semester of academic session 2009-2010. The first half of academic year 2009-2010 was overseen by faculty from IIT Delhi.  IIT Ropar has also been in talks with three of the United Kingdom's best universities.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe UK institutes, with being quite impressed by the state of art facilities at IIT Ropar, have extended their support by signing MoU's in various directions.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Director of the institute, Prof. M.K. Surappa, along with HRD minister Mr. Kapil Sibbal formally visited the universities in UK to share experiences, with their response reciprocated by a senior official from UK visiting the campus in the month of February.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tStudents of the 2008 batch have had a great opportunity to explore their academic abilities under the able guidance of collaborated UK universities in the months of May\u2013June, 2010.<ref>http://www1.aston.ac.uk/international-students/international-news/news-archive/july-2010/aston-university-welcomes-iit-ropar-students/</ref>\n\t\t\t\t\tThe students of the 2008 batch are currently (for the summer period of 2011, May-July) undergoing Industrial Training & Research at various leading industries, companies and other research institutes (such as Microsoft, Bell Labs, Aston University-UK, CSIO-India, Bharti Airtel, Hero Honda, Maruti Suzuki, etc.) in their respective fields. The 2009 batch, now moving to their third academic year (2011-2012) are pursuing their interests through research programmes in various institutes (including Aston University, UK) for the same summer period.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Collaborations in hand and the future plans==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar is keen to start collaborative ventures with universities, industries, and other research institutes (both in India and outside India). In sequel to the agreement signed between the Prime Minister of India and its counterpart in UK in June 2008, a number of universities and their consortia have expressed keen interest in collaborating with IIT Ropar. In the last few months, the Director, Prof. Surappa, has signed a number of MOUs with his counterparts in various universities in the United Kingdom. They have also had several visitors from universities abroad with a view to establish partnership in research and teaching.<ref>http://www.indianexpress.com/news/uk-tieup-on-cards-for-iiserpune-iitpunja/559079/</ref><ref>http://www.ukieri.org/Minister-Pat-McFadden-visit-Feb2010.htm</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Research or inspiration from the innovation==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute, apart from establishing robust teaching environment, is keen to facilitate and support cutting-edge research in a variety of areas. This aspect will enable the students to acquaint themselves with latest development in their respective areas of study and pursue their own research interests. This would also result in a constant revision of the contents of courses that are being taught.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute encourages its faculty members to initiate research work and provides an initiation grant and also the basic facilities for its sustenance. It also encourages faculty members to establish collaborative research ventures with other research lab and industry. In this regard, the institute is keen to establish Central Research Facility. The institute has already started its PhD programme, so that the research environment is further augmented, expanded, and made even more vibrant.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus life/Infrastructure==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Hostel Facilities===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Institute campus houses four hostels: three for boys and one for girls. The hostels are well equipped for comfortable lodging and boarding of approximately 380 students. All hostels are provided with water coolers and RO systems. Each hostel has a common room that provides facilities for indoor recreation and games. The hostel complex also includes four shops that cater to the basic needs of the residents, and also a few washing machine facility. High speed internet is available via wireless internet (spread in the complete campus area) and LAN connections provided by BSNL.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe day-to-day management of hostels is taken care of by a committee consisting of student representatives, faculty members and administrative staff. Each hostel has a warden, who guides the students to manage the affairs of the hostels.\n\t\t\t\t\tInstitute has its own independent post office opened for the staff and students of the institute. SBI (State Bank of India) has a well operational branch inside the campus premises, with talks of ATM being introduced in near early future.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Medical Facility===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute has allocated a separate building, which adjoins the hostel complex, for its medical facility. A doctor and a nurse have been appointed to attend to medical emergencies of the campus residents. In addition the institute relies upon a few super-speciality hospitals in the city of Ropar for providing medical care to its members.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Sports Facilities===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe currently enrollled three batches (2008 entry, 2009 entry and 2010 entry) of students are, apart from showing excellent academic progress, keen to pursue their interests in sports and games. To nurture these interests, the institute has several facilities. At present, the institute has cricket field, three tennis courts, a football field, a hockey field, a gymnasium, a basket ball court and also a number of facilities for several athletic events. The institute also encourages its students to participate in inter-IIT sport events and other competitions. The appointment of a coach has further augmented sports-related activities in the campus.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Students Activity Centre(SAC) has a well equipped gymnasium and supports a music room, available for the students.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Central Library===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Central Library functions as the primary information resource and repository for all teaching and research activities at the institute. Apart from textbooks and recommended reading material prescribed for each course offered at the institute, the library houses a growing collection of research monographs, reports, multi-volume reference works, dictionaries, encyclopedias, handbooks, and so on. In addition, the library also facilitates access to a number of journals through its participation in consortia such as INDEST-AICTE. At present, users can consult more than 4000 books (available on shelves) and hundreds of journals (through electronic subscription).<ref>http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/centrallibrary.shtml</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Security===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute has ensured that its campus and residents are safe and secure. To accomplish this, a security agency has been entrusted with the task of providing security to its personnel and resources.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe beautiful campus has a peaceful environment.<ref>http://picasaweb.google.com/117707137521513270028</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Extra Curricular Activities==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Societies & Clubs===\n\t\t\t\t\tThere are various societies being run by the student body at the institute to promote extra currulicular and co-curricular activities. These clubs ensure participation from the students in different institute level activities & competitions, and prepare them for inter-college competitions. The Music Society, The Dance Club, LitSoc- The Literary Society, The Chess Club, The Athletics Club, The Creative Writing Club, Science and Technology Club, etc. are managed by the respective student representatives and a secretary.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Zeitgeist===\n\t\t\t\t\tZeitgeist is the annual cultural fest of IIT Ropar. The first fest was held in September 2010 and with the theme \"The Spirit of the Times\" (the meaning of the word [[:wikt:Zeitgeist]]).<ref>{{cite web |url= http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/city/chandigarh/Ropar-IIT-gets-its-cultural-icon/articleshow/6674627.cms |title=Ropar IIT gets its cultural icon - The Times of India|work=indiatimes.com  |accessdate=11 October 2011}}</ref> It was sponsored by Hero Honda and the star performers were Faridkot, The Band.{{cn|date=October 2011}} The student body at IIT Ropar aims for the next Zeitgeist to be held in November 2011.{{cn|date=October 2011}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==See also==\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[List of universities in India]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[Indian Institutes of Technology]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[Education in
