It is one of the eight new [[Indian Institutes of Technology]] (IITs) established by the  [[Ministry of Human Resource Development (India)|Ministry of Human Resource Development]] MHRD, Government of India under [[The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Act, 2011]] which declares these eight IITs as well as the conversion of [[Institute of Technology, Banaras Hindu University]] to IIT.<ref name=AmendmentAct>{{cite web|url=http://www.prsindia.org/uploads/media/Institute%20of%20Technology%20Bill%202010.pdf|format=PDF|title=The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Bill, 2010| date = 23 August 2010}}</ref> The Act was passed in the [[Lok Sabha]] on 24 March 2011<ref>{{cite news |url= http://www.deccanherald.com/content/148456/ls-passes-bill-provide-iit.html |title=LS passes bill to provide IIT status to 8 institutes, BHU  |newspaper=Deccan Herald |date=24 March 2011 |accessdate=9 May 2011 | location = New Delhi}}</ref> and by the [[Rajya Sabha]] on 30 April 2012.<ref>{{cite news |url= http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/tech/careers/education/Parliament-passes-IIT-bill/articleshow/12937917.cms |title=Parliament passes IIT bill |newspaper=The Times of India |date=30 April 2012 |accessdate=30 April 2012}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==History==\n\t\t\t\t\tThis new institute was established by MHRD in year 2008. The classes for academic session 2008\u20132009 were held at [[IIT Delhi]]. The Institute started functioning from its transit campus in Rupnagar in August 2009.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://twocircles.net/2009aug07/iit_punjab_start_working_its_new_campus_aug_20.html |title=IIT Punjab to start working from its new campus Aug 20 |author = IANS/Indo-Asian News Service | publisher=TwoCircles.net |date=7 August 2009 | location = New Delhi |accessdate=2013-02-06}}</ref><ref>{{cite news| url=http://articles.timesofindia.indiatimes.com/2009-07-21/india/28211741_1_transit-campus-ropar-iit-delhi | work=The Times of India | title=Big milestone: IIT-Punjab classes from August 20 | date=21 July 2009}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus & Location==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar is located at [[Rupnagar]] (formerly known as Ropar) town of the [[Rupnagar district|district Rupnagar]]. Rupnagar was founded in the 11th century and named after Rup Sen son of Raja Rokeshar. Recent excavations and explorations conducted at Rupnagar indicate that the first settlements here were the [[Indus Valley Civilization|Harappans]], who reached the upper [[Satluj]] towards the close of third millennium B.C. The district has rich historical and religious significance.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tRupnagar town is the headquarters of district Rupnagar and is located 42&nbsp;km. from [[Chandigarh]], the state capital. It is connected by road on [[Indian National Highways|National Highway]] [[NH-21]]. The [[Delhi]]-[[Ambala]]-[[Una, Himachal Pradesh|Una]] railway line passes through Rupnagar and provides rail connectivity. The nearest airport is at Chandigarh at a distance of about 60&nbsp;km. The [[Satluj]] river passes close to Rupnagar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe climate is characterised by its general dryness, except during the south-west monsoon season, a hot summer and a cold winter. The winter is from mid-November to February, summer from March to June and the monsoon from late June to mid-September. The average annual rainfall in the district is about 776&nbsp;mm with about 78% in the period of June to September.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Permanent campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe location for permanent campus of IIT Ropar is Birla Seed Farms, Rupnagar. The Government of Punjab has approved about {{convert|525|acre|km2}} land for the permanent campus in Rupnagar. Foundation stone for the permanent campus of IIT Ropar was laid down on 24 February 2009 by former Union HRD Minister [[Arjun Singh|Mr. Arjun Singh]]. The contract is given to CPWD and a Bangkok-based construction company is assigned the task of finishing the first phase. \n\t\t\t\t\t[[File:IIT Ropar - Main Building of the Transit Campus.JPG|thumbnail|right|IIT ropar transit campus]]\n\t\t\t\t\t<!-- [[Image:IIT ROPAR.jpg|thumb|right|Temporary campus]] -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Temporary campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe temporary campus of IIT Ropar is former Women's Polytechnic, Rupnagar. The academic and administration buildings of the Women's Polytechnic were completely renovated to accommodate all the requirements of the Institute . It has all the basic infrastructure to run Academic programmes specially designed by IIT Delhi. The transit campus is equipped with state of art lecture halls along with well \n\t\t\t\t\tmaintained playgrounds to nurture the bright minds and enhance their overall development. Special emphasis has been laid to set up advanced laboratories to help students gain practical insight of the courses that are a part of their curriculum.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe current temporary campus is a brief 1&nbsp;km walk from Rupnagar railway station.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic system==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe curriculum followed at IIT Ropar provides for a science-based engineering education, with a view to produce quality engineer-scientists. If facilitates broad-based knowledge acquisition and, simultaneously, nurtures a temper for lifelong learning and exploration. Students are encouraged to go beyond the classroom to conduct and carry out independent work by means of research projects, guided reading, and by allowing them to join the research activities undertaken by faculty members. The idea behind such a fashioning of the curriculum is the belief that classroom activities must be supplemented by independent study and also by individual research that broadens one's horizon and provides for opportunities to bring one's ideas to fruition.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe academic programme at the institute follows a semester-based credit system. The prominent feature of the credit system is the process of continuous evaluation of a student's performance and the flexibility to allow a student to progress at an optimum pace suited to his/her ability or convenience, subject to fulfilling minimum requirements for continuation. A minimum Grade Point Average (GPA) is necessary for satisfactory progress and continuation in the programme.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Departments==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute flagged its beginning with the following 7 departments including 3 engineering departments, and 4 supporting departments all of which offer PhD programme.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t* Chemistry\n\t\t\t\t\t* Computer Science & Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Electrical Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Humanities and Social Sciences\n\t\t\t\t\t* Mathematics\n\t\t\t\t\t* Physics\n\t\t\t\t\t* School of Mechanical, Materials & Energy Engineering\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic programmes==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Bachelor's Degree===\n\n\t\t\t\t\tIn its first year of inception 2008\u20132009, three undergraduate programmes were offered. Admission to these programmes is through the IIT-JEE and students are admitted after completing 10+2 (high-school level) schooling.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Computer Science and Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Electrical Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Mechanical Engineering]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Master's Degree===\n\t\t\t\t\tMaster's degree programme is yet to be started.Its going to be started from the academic year 2015.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===PhD Degree===\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar offers admissions for PhD in Computer Science and Engineering, Mechanical Engineering, Electrical Engineering, [[Physics]], [[Chemistry]], [[Mathematics]] and Philosophy.<ref>{{Cite web| url = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml | archiveurl = http://web.archive.org/web/20120114175809/http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml | archivedate = 14 January 2012 | publisher = Indian Institute of Technology Ropar | title = PhD Admissions | date = January 2012 | accessdate = 6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic information==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute's transit campus developed almost fully by the winter semester of academic session 2009\u20132010. The first half of academic year 2009\u20132010 was overseen by faculty from IIT Delhi.  IIT Ropar now has faculty members for seven different departments and schools functional at the institute.<ref>{{Cite web| url = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/faculty.shtml | archiveurl = http://web.archive.org/web/20120504025030/http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/faculty.shtml | archivedate = 4 May 2012 | publisher = Indian Institute of Technology Ropar | title = Faculty | accessdate = 6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\tStudents of the IIT Ropar have had a great opportunities to explore their research capabilities under the able guidance of collaborated UK universities for different Summer sessions.<ref>{{cite web| url = http://www1.aston.ac.uk/international-students/international-news/news-archive/july-2010/aston-university-welcomes-iit-ropar-students/ | title = Aston University welcomes IIT Ropar students | archiveurl = http://web.archive.org/web/20110314234236/http://www1.aston.ac.uk/international-students/international-news/news-archive/july-2010/aston-university-welcomes-iit-ropar-students/ | archivedate = 14 March 2011 | publisher = Aston University | accessdate = 6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Research==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute, apart from establishing robust teaching environment, is keen to facilitate and support cutting-edge research in a variety of areas. This aspect will enable the students to acquaint themselves with latest development in their respective areas of study and pursue their own research interests. This would also result in a constant revision of the contents of courses that are being taught.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute encourages its faculty members to initiate research work and provides an initiation grant and also the basic facilities for its sustenance. It also encourages faculty members to establish collaborative research ventures with other research lab and industry. In this regard, the institute is keen to establish Central Research Facility. The institute has already started its PhD programme, so that the research environment is further augmented, expanded, and made even more vibrant.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus life/Infrastructure==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Hostel Facilities===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Institute campus houses five hostels: four for boys (Mercury Wings A & B, Jupiter and Neptune Houses) and one for girls (Venus House). The hostels are well equipped for comfortable lodging and boarding of approximately 550 students. All hostels are provided with water coolers and RO water filter systems. Each hostel has a common room that provides facilities for indoor recreation and games. The hostel complex also includes two laundry centers. High speed internet is available via wireless internet (spread in the complete campus area) and LAN connections provided by BSNL India.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe day-to-day management of hostels is taken care of by a committee consisting of student representatives, faculty members (as Wardens) and administrative staff (caretakers, office-heads).\n\t\t\t\t\tInstitute has its own independent post office opened for the staff and students of the institute. SBI (State Bank of India) has a well operational branch inside the campus premises.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Medical Facility===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute has allocated a separate building, which adjoins the hostel complex, for its medical facility. A doctor and a nurse have been appointed to attend to medical emergencies of the campus residents. In addition the institute relies upon a few super-speciality hospitals in the city of Ropar for providing medical care to its members.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Image:Iit rpr.jpg|right|thumb|Football field at IIT Ropar]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Sports Facilities===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe students of the institute, apart from showing excellent academic progress, are keen to pursue their interests in sports and games. To nurture these interests, the institute provides several facilities. At present, the institute has a cricket field, three tennis courts, a football field, a hockey field, a gymnasium, a basketball court, a volleyball court and also a number of facilities for several athletics.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute also encourages its students to participate in the inter-IIT competition which is held every year in December at different IIT campuses across India and other competitions.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Students Activity Center (SAC) has a well equipped gymnasium and rooms for different activity clubs such as the Music Club, Dance Club and the Fine Arts Club.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Central Library===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Central Library functions as the primary information resource and repository for all teaching and research activities at the institute. Apart from textbooks and recommended reading material prescribed for each course offered at the institute, the library houses a growing collection of research monographs, reports, multi-volume reference works, dictionaries, encyclopaedias, handbooks, and so on. In addition, the library also facilitates access to a number of journals through its participation in consortia such as INDEST-AICTE. At present, users can consult more than 4000 books (available on shelves) and hundreds of journals (through electronic subscription).<ref>{{cite web| url = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/centrallibrary.shtml | archiveurl = http://web.archive.org/web/20120504024741/http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/centrallibrary.shtml | archivedate = 4 May 2012 | title = Central Library | publisher = Indian Institute of Technology Ropar | accessdate = 6 February 2013 }}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Security===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute has ensured that its campus and residents are safe and secure. To accomplish this, a security agency has been entrusted with the task of providing security to its personnel and resources.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe beautiful campus has a peaceful environment.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://picasaweb.google.com/117707137521513270028 |publisher = Picasa Web Albums | title = IIT Ropar's Gallery (7 Albums) |date=8 May 2010 |accessdate=6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Extra Curricular Activities==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Societies & Clubs===\n\t\t\t\t\tThere are various societies being run by the student body at the institute to promote extra currulicular and co-curricular activities. These clubs ensure participation from the students in different institute level activities & competitions, and prepare them for inter-college competitions. The Fine Arts Club, The Music Society, The Dance Club, LitSoc- The Literary Society, The Chess Club, The Athletics Club, The Creative Writing Club, Science and Technology Club, etc. are managed by the respective student representatives and a secretary.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t====Music Society====\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Music Society provides performance opportunities and brings live music to events during the academic year. Anyone who has an interest in playing an instrument, singing or appreciating music is welcome to join. In the Student Activity Center, is a music room with various instruments including a complete drum set, acoustic and electric guitars, and a keyboard. All details regarding this society can be found at http://iitrprmusicsociety.webs.com/\n\n\t\t\t\t\t=====Events held=====\n\t\t\t\t\t*Saaz \u2013 Solo singing competition\n\t\t\t\t\t*Sur \u2013 Duet singing competition\n\t\t\t\t\t*Rashmi - Kavi Sammelan \n\t\t\t\t\t*Torque \u2013 Rock band competition (Part of Zeitgeist)\n\t\t\t\t\t*Symphony \u2013 Western instrumental competition (Part of Zeitgeist)\n\t\t\t\t\t*Raag \u2013 Indian instrumental competition (Part of Zeitgeist)\n\t\t\t\t\t*Zeitgeist - cultural and tech festival\n\t\t\t\t\t*Samagam - weekend cultural acitivities\n\t\t\t\t\t*Conclave - English debate\n\t\t\t\t\t*Viruddh - Hindi debate .\n\n\t\t\t\t\t====Alumni Association====\n\t\t\t\t\tThe IIT Ropar Alumni Association is an association for the 300+ alumni of the institute. It has an office at the campus.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==See also==\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[List of universities in India]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[Indian Institutes of Technology]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[Education in India]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==References==\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Reflist}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==External links==\n\t\t\t\t\t* [http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/ IIT Ropar (Punjab) official website]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [https://plus.google.com/+iitropar IIT Ropar on Google+]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [https://www.facebook.com/iitropar IIT Ropar Students on Facebook]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Indian Institute Of Technology}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t{{DEFAULTSORT:Indian Institute Of Technology Punjab}}\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Indian Institutes of Technology|Ropar]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Technical universities and colleges]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Educational institutions established in 2008]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Rupnagar]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Engineering colleges in Punjab, India]]\n\t\t\t\t"}, {"text": "-1 `\t\t{{about|a technology institute in [[Ropar|Ropar, India]]|the similarly named institutes |Indian Institute of Technology (disambiguation)}}`\t\t{{Use 2232 "}, {"text": "2246 "}, {"text": "256 -1 (IITs)<ref>{{cite web|title=IIT Ropar is now independent of IIT Delhi's mentoring and administration|url=http://economictimes.indiatimes.com/industry/services/education/iit^ropar^is^now^independent^of^iit^delhis^mentoring^and^administration/articleshow/48217835.cms}}</ref> 1989 "}, {"text": "132 -2 Prof. Javagal K. Sridhar\n\t\t\t\t\t}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe '''Indian Institute of Technology Ropar''' ('''IIT Ropar''') or '''IIT-RPR''', is an engineering and technology higher education institute located in [[Rupnagar]], [[Punjab, India|Punjab]], India. It is one of the eight newer [[Indian Institutes of Technology]] (IITs)<ref>{{cite web|title=IIT Ropar is now independent of IIT Delhi's mentoring and administration|url=http://economictimes.indiatimes.com/industry/services/education/iit-ropar-is-now-independent-of-iit-delhis-mentoring-and-administration/articleshow/48217835.cms}}</ref> established by the  [[Ministry of Human Resource Development (India)|Ministry of Human Resource Development]] MHRD, Government of India under [[The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Act, 2011]].<ref name=AmendmentAct>{{cite web|url=http://www.prsindia.org/uploads/media/Institute%20of%20Technology%20Bill%202010.pdf|format=PDF|title=The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Bill, 2010| date = 23 August 2010}}</ref> The Act was passed in the [[Lok Sabha]] on 24 March 2011<ref>{{cite news |url= http://www.deccanherald.com/content/148456/ls-passes-bill-provide-iit.html |title=LS passes bill to provide IIT status to 8 institutes, BHU  |newspaper=Deccan Herald |date=24 March 2011 |accessdate=9 May 2011 | location = New Delhi}}</ref> and by the [[Rajya Sabha]] on 30 April 2012.<ref>{{cite news |url= http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/tech/careers/education/Parliament-passes-IIT-bill/articleshow/12937917.cms |title=Parliament passes IIT bill |newspaper=The Times of India |date=30 April 2012 |accessdate=30 April 2012}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==History==\n\t\t\t\t\tThis new institute was established by MHRD in year 2008. The classes for academic session 2008\u20132009 were held at [[IIT Delhi]]. The Institute started functioning from its transit campus in Rupnagar in August 2009.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://twocircles.net/2009aug07/iit_punjab_start_working_its_new_campus_aug_20.html |title=IIT Punjab to start working from its new campus Aug 20 |author = IANS/Indo-Asian News Service | publisher=TwoCircles.net |date=7 August 2009 | location = New Delhi |accessdate=2013-02-06}}</ref><ref>{{cite news| url=http://articles.timesofindia.indiatimes.com/2009-07-21/india/28211741_1_transit-campus-ropar-iit-delhi | work=The Times of India | title=Big milestone: IIT-Punjab classes from August 20 | date=21 July 2009}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus & Location==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar is located at [[Rupnagar]] (formerly known as Ropar) town of the [[Rupnagar district|district Rupnagar]]. Rupnagar was founded in the 11th century and named after Rup Sen son of Raja Rokeshar. Recent excavations and explorations conducted at Rupnagar indicate that the first settlements here were the [[Indus Valley Civilization|Harappans]], who reached the upper [[Satluj]] towards the close of third millennium B.C. The district has rich historical and religious significance.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tRupnagar town is the headquarters of district Rupnagar and is located 42&nbsp;km. from [[Chandigarh]], the state capital. It is connected by road on [[Indian National Highways|National Highway]] [[NH-21]]. The [[Delhi]]-[[Ambala]]-[[Una, Himachal Pradesh|Una]] railway line passes through Rupnagar and provides rail connectivity. The nearest airport is at Chandigarh at a distance of about 60&nbsp;km. The [[Satluj]] river passes close to Rupnagar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe climate is characterised by its general dryness, except during the south-west monsoon season, a hot summer and a cold winter. The winter is from mid-November to February, summer from March to June and the monsoon from late June to mid-September. The average annual rainfall in the district is about 776&nbsp;mm with about 78% in the period of June to September.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Permanent campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe location for permanent campus of IIT Ropar is Birla Seed Farms, Rupnagar. The Government of Punjab has approved about {{convert|525|acre|km2}} land for the permanent campus in Rupnagar. Foundation stone for the permanent campus of IIT Ropar was laid down on 24 February 2009 by former Union HRD Minister [[Arjun Singh|Mr. Arjun Singh]]. The contract is given to CPWD and a Bangkok-based construction company is assigned the task of finishing the first phase. \n\t\t\t\t\t[[File:IIT Ropar - Main Building of the Transit Campus.JPG|thumbnail|IIT Ropar transit campus]]\n\t\t\t\t\t<!-- [[Image:IIT ROPAR.jpg|thumb|right|Temporary campus]] -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Temporary campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe temporary campus of IIT Ropar is former Women's Polytechnic, Rupnagar. The academic and administration buildings of the Women's Polytechnic were completely renovated to accommodate all the requirements of the Institute . It has all the basic infrastructure to run Academic programmes specially designed by IIT Delhi. The transit campus is equipped with state of art lecture halls along with well \n\t\t\t\t\tmaintained playgrounds to nurture the bright minds and enhance their overall development. Special emphasis has been laid to set up advanced laboratories to help students gain practical insight of the courses that are a part of their curriculum.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe current temporary campus is a brief 1&nbsp;km walk from Rupnagar railway station.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic system==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe curriculum followed at IIT Ropar provides for a science-based engineering education, with a view to produce quality engineer-scientists. If facilitates broad-based knowledge acquisition and, simultaneously, nurtures a temper for lifelong learning and exploration. Students are encouraged to go beyond the classroom to conduct and carry out independent work by means of research projects, guided reading, and by allowing them to join the research activities undertaken by faculty members. The idea behind such a fashioning of the curriculum is the belief that classroom activities must be supplemented by independent study and also by individual research that broadens one's horizon and provides for opportunities to bring one's ideas to fruition.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe academic programme at the institute follows a semester-based credit system. The prominent feature of the credit system is the process of continuous evaluation of a student's performance and the flexibility to allow a student to progress at an optimum pace suited to his/her ability or convenience, subject to fulfilling minimum requirements for continuation. A minimum Grade Point Average (GPA) is necessary for satisfactory progress and continuation in the programme.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Rankings===\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Infobox India university ranking\n\t\t\t\t\t| Ministry of Human Resource Development in April 2016.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Departments==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute flagged its beginning with the following 9 departments including 4 engineering departments, and 5 supporting departments all of which offer PhD programme.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t* [http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/cbme Center for Biomedical Engineering (CBME)]\n\t\t\t\t\t* Center for Materials and Energy Sciences]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/mathematics Mathematics]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/smmee Mechanical Engineering]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/physics Physics]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic Programmes==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Bachelor's Degree===\n\n\t\t\t\t\tIn its first year of inception 2008\u20132009, three undergraduate programmes were offered. Admission to these programmes is through the JEE Advanced and students are admitted after completing 10+2 (high-school level) schooling.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Computer Science and Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Electrical Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Mechanical Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Civil Engineering]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Master's Degree===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute provides Master's degree M.Tech. in Mechanical Engineering, M.S. in Chemistry, Physics, Mathematics and Linguistics\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===PhD Degree===\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar offers admissions for PhD in Computer Science and Engineering, Mechanical Engineering, Electrical Engineering, [[Physics]], [[Chemistry]], [[Mathematics]] and Philosophy.<ref>{{Cite web| url = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20120114175809/http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml | archivedate = 14 January 2012 | publisher = Indian Institute of Technology Ropar | title = PhD Admissions | date = January 2012 | accessdate = 6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic information==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute's transit campus developed almost fully by the winter semester of academic session 2009\u20132010. The first half of academic year 2009\u20132010 was overseen by faculty from IIT Delhi.  IIT Ropar now has faculty members for seven different departments and schools functional at the institute.<ref>{{Cite web| url = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/faculty.shtml | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20120504025030/http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/faculty.shtml | archivedate = 4 May 2012 | publisher = Indian Institute of Technology Ropar | title = Faculty | accessdate = 6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\tStudents of the IIT Ropar have had a great opportunities to explore their research capabilities under the able guidance of collaborated UK universities for different Summer sessions.<ref>{{cite web| url = http://www1.aston.ac.uk/international-students/international-news/news-archive/july-2010/aston-university-welcomes-iit-ropar-students/ | title = Aston University welcomes IIT Ropar students | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20110314234236/http://www1.aston.ac.uk/international-students/international-news/news-archive/july-2010/aston-university-welcomes-iit-ropar-students/ | archivedate = 14 March 2011 | publisher = Aston University | accessdate = 6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Research==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute, apart from establishing robust teaching environment, is keen to facilitate and support cutting-edge research in a variety of areas. This aspect will enable the students to acquaint themselves with latest development in their respective areas of study and pursue their own research interests. This would also result in a constant revision of the contents of courses that are being taught.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute encourages its faculty members to initiate research work and provides an initiation grant and also the basic facilities for its sustenance. It also encourages faculty members to establish collaborative research ventures with other research lab and industry. In this regard, the institute is keen to establish Central Research Facility. The institute has already started its PhD programme, so that the research environment is further augmented, expanded, and made even more vibrant.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus life/Infrastructure==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Hostel Facilities===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Institute campus houses five hostels: four for boys (Mercury Wings A , B & C, Jupiter and Neptune Houses) and one for girls (Venus House). The hostels are well equipped for comfortable lodging and boarding of approximately 550 students. All hostels are provided with water coolers and RO water filter systems. Each hostel has a common room that provides facilities for indoor recreation and games. The hostel complex also includes two laundry centers. High speed internet is available via wireless internet (spread in the complete campus area) and LAN connections provided by BSNL India.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe day-to-day management of hostels is taken care of by a committee consisting of student representatives, faculty members (as Wardens) and administrative staff (caretakers, office-heads).\n\t\t\t\t\tInstitute has its own independent post office opened for the staff and students of the institute. SBI (State Bank of India) has a well operational branch inside the campus premises.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Medical Facility===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute has allocated a separate building, which adjoins the hostel complex, for its medical facility. A doctor and a nurse have been appointed to attend to medical emergencies of the campus residents. In addition the institute relies upon a few super-speciality hospitals in the city of Ropar for providing medical care to its members.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Image:Iit rpr.jpg|right|thumb|Football field at IIT Ropar]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Sports Facilities===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe students of the institute, apart from showing excellent academic progress, are keen to pursue their interests in sports and games. To nurture these interests, the institute provides several facilities. At present, the institute has a cricket field, three tennis courts, a football field, a gymnasium, a basketball court, two volleyball court and also a number of facilities for several athletics.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute also encourages its students to participate in the inter-IIT competition which is held every year in December at different IIT campuses across India and other competitions.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Students Activity Center (SAC) has a well equipped gymnasium and rooms for different activity clubs such as the Music Club, Dance Club and the Fine Arts Club.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Central Library===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Central Library functions as the primary information resource and repository for all teaching and research activities at the institute. Apart from textbooks and recommended reading material prescribed for each course offered at the institute, the library houses a growing collection of research monographs, reports, multi-volume reference works, dictionaries, encyclopaedias, handbooks, and so on. In addition, the library also facilitates access to a number of journals through its participation in consortia such as INDEST-AICTE. At present, users can consult more than 4000 books (available on shelves) and hundreds of journals (through electronic subscription).<ref>{{cite web| url = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/centrallibrary.shtml | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20120504024741/http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/centrallibrary.shtml | archivedate = 4 May 2012 | title = Central Library | publisher = Indian Institute of Technology Ropar | accessdate = 6 February 2013 }}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Security===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute has ensured that its campus and residents are safe and secure. To accomplish this, a security agency has been entrusted with the task of providing security to its personnel and resources.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe beautiful campus has a peaceful environment.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://picasaweb.google.com/117707137521513270028 |publisher = Picasa Web Albums | title = IIT Ropar's Gallery (7 Albums) |date=8 May 2010 |accessdate=6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Extra Curricular Activities==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Societies & Clubs===\n\t\t\t\t\tThere are various societies being run by the student body at the institute to promote extra currulicular and co-curricular activities. These clubs ensure participation from the students in different institute level activities & competitions, and prepare them for inter-college competitions. The Fine Arts Club, The Music Society, The Dance Club, LitSoc- The Literary Society, The Chess Club, The Athletics Club, The Creative Writing Club, Science and Technology Club, etc. are managed by the respective student representatives and a secretary.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Zeitgiest===\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Zeitgeist (festival)| Zeitgeist]] is the annual cultural festival of Indian Institute of Technology Ropar and is held annually as a three-day festival in late Feb - early March. It was conceived in September 2010.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zeitgeist_(festival) |title=Zeitgeist IIT Ropar}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t====Music Society====\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Music Society provides performance opportunities and brings live music to events during the academic year. Anyone who has an interest in playing an instrument, singing or appreciating music is welcome to join. In the Student Activity Center, is a music room with various instruments including a complete drum set, acoustic and electric guitars, and a keyboard. All details regarding this society can be found at http://iitrprmusicsociety.webs.com/\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==== Inter Batch Cultural Championship ====\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Inter Batch Cultural Championship or IBCC is the inter batch cultural competition of IIT Ropar and was inaugurated in 2014 to instil competitiveness amongst the students. Dance, music, and art are included in the list of events.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t=====Events held=====\n\t\t\t\t\t*Saaz \u2013 Solo singing competition\n\t\t\t\t\t*Sur \u2013 Duet singing competition\n\t\t\t\t\t*Rashmi - Kavi Sammelan \n\t\t\t\t\t*Torque \u2013 Rock band competition (Part of [[Zeitgeist (festival)| Zeitgeist]])\n\t\t\t\t\t*Symphony \u2013 Western instrumental competition (Part of [[Zeitgeist (festival)| Zeitgeist]])\n\t\t\t\t\t*Raag \u2013 Indian instrumental competition (Part of [[Zeitgeist (festival)| Zeitgeist]])\n\t\t\t\t\t*[[Zeitgeist (festival)| Zeitgeist]] - cultural festival\n\t\t\t\t\t*Samagam - weekend cultural activities\n\t\t\t\t\t*Conclave - English debate\n\t\t\t\t\t*Viruddh - Hindi debate .\n\n\t\t\t\t\t====Alumni Association====\n\t\t\t\t\tThe IIT Ropar Alumni Association was founded on 1st February 2013. The Association aims to encourage the Alumni to take abiding interest in the progress and development of the Institute. Since its establishment, the Association has grown from strength to strength, regularly undertaking several initiatives to promote and foster mutually beneficial interaction between the Alumni and the Alma Mater.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://alumni.iitrpr.ac.in |title=IIT Ropar Alumni Association}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\tVisit [http://alumni.iitrpr.ac.in Official Website] for more info\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==See also==\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[List of universities in India]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[Indian Institutes of Technology]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[Education in India]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==References==\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Reflist}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==External links==\n\t\t\t\t\t* [http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/ IIT Ropar (Punjab) official website]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [https://plus.google.com/+iitropar IIT Ropar on Google+]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [https://www.facebook.com/iitropar IIT Ropar Students on Facebook]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Indian Institute Of Technology}}\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Authority Control}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t{{DEFAULTSORT:Indian Institute Of Technology Punjab}}\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Indian Institutes of Technology|Ropar]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Technical universities and colleges]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Educational institutions established in 2008]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Rupnagar]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Engineering colleges in Punjab, India]]\n\t\t\t\t"}, {"text": "1098 -1 '10' 6 -1 '6' 1359 "}, {"text": "1120 [http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/smmee 5 -1 Engineering (CMEE)]`\t\t* 1339 "}, {"text": "41 -1 \u0927\u093f\u092f\u094b 2425 "}, {"text": "44 -1 \u092a\u094d\u0930\u091a\u094b\u0926\u092f\u093e\u0924\u094d`\t\t| 2422 "}, {"text": "19 -2 2013}}`\t\t{{Infobox 2446 "}, {"text": "2060 -1 Activities==``\t\t===Zeitgiest===`\t\t[[Zeitgeist (festival)| Zeitgeist]] is the annual cultural festival of Indian Institute of Technology Ropar and is held annually as a three^day festival in late Feb ^ early March. It is one of the eight newer [[Indian Institutes of Technology]] (IITs)<ref>{{cite web|title=IIT Ropar is now independent of IIT Delhi's mentoring and administration|url=http://economictimes.indiatimes.com/industry/services/education/iit-ropar-is-now-independent-of-iit-delhis-mentoring-and-administration/articleshow/48217835.cms}}</ref> established by the  [[Ministry of Human Resource Development (India)|Ministry of Human Resource Development]] MHRD, Government of India under The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Act, 2011.<ref name=AmendmentAct>{{cite web|url=http://www.prsindia.org/uploads/media/Institute%20of%20Technology%20Bill%202010.pdf|format=PDF|title=The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Bill, 2010| date = 23 August 2010}}</ref> The Act was passed in the [[Lok Sabha]] on 24 March 2011<ref>{{cite news |url= http://www.deccanherald.com/content/148456/ls-passes-bill-provide-iit.html |title=LS passes bill to provide IIT status to 8 institutes, BHU  |newspaper=Deccan Herald |date=24 March 2011 |accessdate=9 May 2011 | location = New Delhi}}</ref> and by the [[Rajya Sabha]] on 30 April 2012.<ref>{{cite news |url= http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/tech/careers/education/Parliament-passes-IIT-bill/articleshow/12937917.cms |title=Parliament passes IIT bill |newspaper=The Times of India |date=30 April 2012 |accessdate=30 April 2012}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==History==\n\t\t\t\t\tThis new institute was established by MHRD in year 2008. The classes for academic session 2008\u20132009 were held at [[IIT Delhi]]. The Institute started functioning from its transit campus in Rupnagar in August 2009.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://twocircles.net/2009aug07/iit_punjab_start_working_its_new_campus_aug_20.html |title=IIT Punjab to start working from its new campus Aug 20 |author = IANS/Indo-Asian News Service | publisher=TwoCircles.net |date=7 August 2009 | location = New Delhi |accessdate=2013-02-06}}</ref><ref>{{cite news| url=http://articles.timesofindia.indiatimes.com/2009-07-21/india/28211741_1_transit-campus-ropar-iit-delhi | work=The Times of India | title=Big milestone: IIT-Punjab classes from August 20 | date=21 July 2009}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus & Location==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar is located at [[Rupnagar]] (formerly known as Ropar) town of the [[Rupnagar district|district Rupnagar]]. Rupnagar was founded in the 11th century and named after Rup Sen son of Raja Rokeshar. Recent excavations and explorations conducted at Rupnagar indicate that the first settlements here were the [[Indus Valley Civilization|Harappans]], who reached the upper [[Satluj]] towards the close of third millennium B.C. The district has rich historical and religious significance.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tRupnagar town is the headquarters of district Rupnagar and is located 42&nbsp;km. from [[Chandigarh]], the state capital. It is connected by road on [[Indian National Highways|National Highway]] [[NH-21]]. The [[Delhi]]-[[Ambala]]-[[Una, Himachal Pradesh|Una]] railway line passes through Rupnagar and provides rail connectivity. The nearest airport is at Chandigarh at a distance of about 60&nbsp;km. The [[Satluj]] river passes close to Rupnagar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe climate is characterised by its general dryness, except during the south-west monsoon season, a hot summer and a cold winter. The winter is from mid-November to February, summer from March to June and the monsoon from late June to mid-September. The average annual rainfall in the district is about 776&nbsp;mm with about 78% in the period of June to September.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Permanent campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe location for permanent campus of IIT Ropar is Birla Seed Farms, Rupnagar. The Government of Punjab has approved about {{convert|525|acre|km2}} land for the permanent campus in Rupnagar. Foundation stone for the permanent campus of IIT Ropar was laid down on 24 February 2009 by former Union HRD Minister [[Arjun Singh|Mr. Arjun Singh]]. The contract is given to CPWD and a Bangkok-based construction company is assigned the task of finishing the first phase. \n\t\t\t\t\t[[File:IIT Ropar - Main Building of the Transit Campus.JPG|thumbnail|IIT Ropar transit campus]]\n\t\t\t\t\t<!-- [[File:IIT ROPAR.jpg|thumb|right|Temporary campus]] -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Temporary campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe temporary campus of IIT Ropar is former Women's Polytechnic, Rupnagar. The academic and administration buildings of the Women's Polytechnic were completely renovated to accommodate all the requirements of the Institute . It has all the basic infrastructure to run Academic programmes specially designed by IIT Delhi. The transit campus is equipped with state of art lecture halls along with well \n\t\t\t\t\tmaintained playgrounds to nurture the bright minds and enhance their overall development. Special emphasis has been laid to set up advanced laboratories to help students gain practical insight of the courses that are a part of their curriculum.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe current temporary campus is a brief 1&nbsp;km walk from Rupnagar railway station.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic system==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe curriculum followed at IIT Ropar provides for a science-based engineering education, with a view to produce quality engineer-scientists. If facilitates broad-based knowledge acquisition and, simultaneously, nurtures a temper for lifelong learning and exploration. Students are encouraged to go beyond the classroom to conduct and carry out independent work by means of research projects, guided reading, and by allowing them to join the research activities undertaken by faculty members. The idea behind such a fashioning of the curriculum is the belief that classroom activities must be supplemented by independent study and also by individual research that broadens one's horizon and provides for opportunities to bring one's ideas to fruition.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe academic programme at the institute follows a semester-based credit system. The prominent feature of the credit system is the process of continuous evaluation of a student's performance and the flexibility to allow a student to progress at an optimum pace suited to his/her ability or convenience, subject to fulfilling minimum requirements for continuation. A minimum Grade Point Average (GPA) is necessary for satisfactory progress and continuation in the programme.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Rankings===\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Infobox India university ranking\n\t\t\t\t\t| type = University and college\n\t\t\t\t\t<!----------International---------->\n\t\t\t\t\t| QS_W = \n\t\t\t\t\t| QS_A = \n\t\t\t\t\t| THES_W = \n\t\t\t\t\t| ARWU_W = \n\t\t\t\t\t<!----------General---------->\n\t\t\t\t\t| CAREER_U = \n\t\t\t\t\t<!----------Engineering---------->\n\t\t\t\t\t| NIRF = 21\n\t\t\t\t\t| IT_E = \n\t\t\t\t\t| OUTLOOK = \n\t\t\t\t\t| DQ = \n\t\t\t\t\t| CSR_E = \n\t\t\t\t\t| MINT_P = \n\t\t\t\t\t| MINT_G = \n\t\t\t\t\t| EFY= \n\t\t\t\t\t<!----------Law---------->\n\t\t\t\t\t| IT_L = \n\t\t\t\t\t| MINT_L = \n\t\t\t\t\t<!----------Business---------->\n\t\t\t\t\t| IT_B = \n\t\t\t\t\t| CSR_B =\n\t\t\t\t\t}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar is ranked 21 in ''[[National Institutional Ranking Framework]]'' published by [[Ministry of Human Resource Development]] in April 2017.<ref name=Rankings_NIRF/>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Departments==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute flagged its beginning with the following 10 departments including 4 engineering and 6 science departments, all of which offer PhD programme.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic Programmes==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Bachelor's Degree===\n\n\t\t\t\t\tIn its first year of inception 2008\u20132009, three undergraduate programmes were offered. Admission to these programmes is through the JEE Advanced and students are admitted after completing 10+2 (high-school level) schooling.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Computer Science and Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Electrical Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Mechanical Engineering]]\n\t\t\t\t\t*Bachelor of Technology in [[Civil Engineering]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Master's Degree===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute provides following master's degree \n\n\t\t\t\t\tM.Tech. in \n\t\t\t\t\t* Mechanical Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Electrical Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Computer Science & Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Biomedical Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\tMS (Research) in \n\t\t\t\t\t* Computer Science and Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Electrical Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\tM.Sc in \n\t\t\t\t\t* Chemistry\n\t\t\t\t\t* Physics\n\t\t\t\t\t* Mathematics\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===PhD Degree===\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar offers admissions for PhD in Computer Science and Engineering, Mechanical Engineering, Electrical Engineering, Center for Materials & Energy Engineering, Center for Biomedical Engineering, [[Physics]], [[Chemistry]], [[Mathematics]] and Philosophy.<ref>{{Cite web| url = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20120114175809/http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml | archivedate = 14 January 2012 | publisher = Indian Institute of Technology Ropar | title = PhD Admissions | date = January 2012 | accessdate = 6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academic information==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute's transit campus developed almost fully by the winter semester of academic session 2009\u20132010. The first half of academic year 2009\u20132010 was overseen by faculty from IIT Delhi.  IIT Ropar now has faculty members for seven different departments and schools functional at the institute.<ref>{{Cite web| url = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/faculty.shtml | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20120504025030/http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/faculty.shtml | archivedate = 4 May 2012 | publisher = Indian Institute of Technology Ropar | title = Faculty | accessdate = 6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\tStudents of the IIT Ropar have had a great opportunities to explore their research capabilities under the able guidance of collaborated UK universities for different Summer sessions.<ref>{{cite web| url = http://www1.aston.ac.uk/international-students/international-news/news-archive/july-2010/aston-university-welcomes-iit-ropar-students/ | title = Aston University welcomes IIT Ropar students | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20110314234236/http://www1.aston.ac.uk/international-students/international-news/news-archive/july-2010/aston-university-welcomes-iit-ropar-students/ | archivedate = 14 March 2011 | publisher = Aston University | accessdate = 6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Research==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute, apart from establishing robust teaching environment, is keen to facilitate and support cutting-edge research in a variety of areas. This aspect will enable the students to acquaint themselves with latest development in their respective areas of study and pursue their own research interests. This would also result in a constant revision of the contents of courses that are being taught.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute encourages its faculty members to initiate research work and provides an initiation grant and also the basic facilities for its sustenance. It also encourages faculty members to establish collaborative research ventures with other research lab and industry. In this regard, the institute is keen to establish Central Research Facility. The institute has already started its PhD programme, so that the research environment is further augmented, expanded, and made even more vibrant.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus life/Infrastructure==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Hostel Facilities===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Institute campus houses five hostels: four for boys (Mercury Wings A, B & C, Jupiter and Neptune Houses) and one for girls (Venus House). The hostels are well equipped for comfortable lodging and boarding of approximately 550 students. All hostels are provided with water coolers and RO water filter systems. Each hostel has a common room that provides facilities for indoor recreation and games. The hostel complex also includes two laundry centers. High speed internet is available via wireless internet (spread in the complete campus area) and LAN connections provided by BSNL India.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe day-to-day management of hostels is taken care of by a committee consisting of student representatives, faculty members (as Wardens) and administrative staff (caretakers, office-heads).\n\t\t\t\t\tInstitute has its own independent post office opened for the staff and students of the institute. SBI (State Bank of India) has a well operational branch inside the campus premises.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Medical Facility===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute has allocated a separate building, which adjoins the hostel complex, for its medical facility. A doctor and a nurse have been appointed to attend to medical emergencies of the campus residents. In addition the institute relies upon a few super-speciality hospitals in the city of Ropar for providing medical care to its members.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t[[File:Iit rpr.jpg|right|thumb|Football field at IIT Ropar]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Sports Facilities===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe students of the institute, apart from showing excellent academic progress, are keen to pursue their interests in sports and games. To nurture these interests, the institute provides several facilities. At present, the institute has a cricket field, three tennis courts, a football field, a gymnasium, a basketball court, two volleyball court and also a number of facilities for several athletics.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute also encourages its students to participate in the inter-IIT competition which is held every year in December at different IIT campuses across India and other competitions.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Students Activity Center (SAC) has a well equipped gymnasium and rooms for different activity clubs such as the Music Club, Dance Club and the Fine Arts Club.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Central Library===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Central Library functions as the primary information resource and repository for all teaching and research activities at the institute. Apart from textbooks and recommended reading material prescribed for each course offered at the institute, the library houses a growing collection of research monographs, reports, multi-volume reference works, dictionaries, encyclopaedias, handbooks, and so on. In addition, the library also facilitates access to a number of journals through its participation in consortia such as INDEST-AICTE. At present, users can consult more than 4000 books (available on shelves) and hundreds of journals (through electronic subscription).<ref>{{cite web| url = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/centrallibrary.shtml | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20120504024741/http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/centrallibrary.shtml | archivedate = 4 May 2012 | title = Central Library | publisher = Indian Institute of Technology Ropar | accessdate = 6 February 2013 }}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Security===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute has ensured that its campus and residents are safe and secure. To accomplish this, a security agency has been entrusted with the task of providing security to its personnel and resources.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe beautiful campus has a peaceful environment.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://picasaweb.google.com/117707137521513270028 |publisher = Picasa Web Albums | title = IIT Ropar's Gallery (7 Albums) |date=8 May 2010 |accessdate=6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Extra Curricular Activities==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Societies & Clubs===\n\t\t\t\t\tThere are various societies being run by the student body at the institute to promote extra currulicular and co-curricular activities. These clubs ensure participation from the students in different institute level activities & competitions, and prepare them for inter-college competitions. The Fine Arts Club, The Music Society, The Dance Club, LitSoc- The Literary Society, The Chess Club, The Athletics Club, The Creative Writing Club, Science and Technology Club, etc. are managed by the respective student representatives and a secretary.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Zeitgeist===\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Zeitgeist (festival)|Zeitgeist]] is the annual cultural festival of Indian Institute of Technology Ropar and is held annually as a three-day festival in late Feb - early March. It was conceived in September 2010.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Advitiya===\n\t\t\t\t\tAdvitiya is the upcoming annual technical festival of Indian Institute of Technology Ropar to be held as a three-day festival in late March. Its maiden edition will be held from 22 March 2017 to 24 March 2017.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Music Society===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Music Society provides performance opportunities and brings live music to events during the academic year. Anyone who has an interest in playing an instrument, singing or appreciating music is welcome to join. In the Student Activity Center, is a music room with various instruments including a complete drum set, acoustic and electric guitars, and a keyboard. All details regarding this society can be found at http://iitrprmusicsociety.webs.com/\n\n\t\t\t\t\t=== Inter Batch Cultural Championship ===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Inter Batch Cultural Championship or IBCC is the inter batch cultural competition of IIT Ropar and was inaugurated in 2014 to instil competitiveness amongst the students. Dance, music, and art are included in the list of events.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Events held===\n\t\t\t\t\t*Saaz \u2013 Solo singing competition\n\t\t\t\t\t*Sur \u2013 Duet singing competition\n\t\t\t\t\t*Rashmi - Kavi Sammelan \n\t\t\t\t\t*Torque \u2013 Rock band competition (Part of [[Zeitgeist (festival)|Zeitgeist]])\n\t\t\t\t\t*Symphony \u2013 Western instrumental competition (Part of [[Zeitgeist (festival)|Zeitgeist]])\n\t\t\t\t\t*Raag \u2013 Indian instrumental competition (Part of [[Zeitgeist (festival)|Zeitgeist]])\n\t\t\t\t\t*[[Zeitgeist (festival)|Zeitgeist]] - cultural festival\n\t\t\t\t\t*Samagam - weekend cultural activities\n\t\t\t\t\t*Conclave - English debate\n\t\t\t\t\t*Viruddh - Hindi debate .\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Alumni Association==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe IIT Ropar Alumni Association was founded on 1 February 2013. The Association aims to encourage the Alumni to take abiding interest in the progress and development of the Institute. Since its establishment, the Association has grown from strength to strength, regularly undertaking several initiatives to promote and foster mutually beneficial interaction between the Alumni and the Alma Mater.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://alumni.iitrpr.ac.in |title=IIT Ropar Alumni Association}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\tVisit [http://alumni.iitrpr.ac.in Official Website] for more info\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==See Raina\n\t\t\t\t\t| director          = Sarit Kumar Das\n\t\t\t\t\t| head_label        =\n\t\t\t\t\t| head              =\n\t\t\t\t\t| academic_staff    =\n\t\t\t\t\t| administrative_staff  =\n\t\t\t\t\t| students          = \n\t\t\t\t\t| undergrad         = \n\t\t\t\t\t| postgrad          = \n\t\t\t\t\t| doctoral          = \n\t\t\t\t\t| other             =\n\t\t\t\t\t| city              = [[Rupnagar]]\n\t\t\t\t\t| state             = [[Punjab, India|Punjab]]\n\t\t\t\t\t| province          =\n\t\t\t\t\t| country           = [[India]]\n\t\t\t\t\t| coor              = {{Coord|30.9755|76.5395|type:edu|display=inline,title}}\n\t\t\t\t\t| campus            = Main \u2013 Spread over {{convert|520|acre|km2}}, Transit \u2013 Spread over {{convert|25|acre|km2}}\n\t\t\t\t\t| former_names      = Indian Institute of Technology Punjab\n\t\t\t\t\t| free_label        =\n\t\t\t\t\t| free              =\n\t\t\t\t\t| athletics         =\n\t\t\t\t\t| colours           =\n\t\t\t\t\t| sports            =\n\t\t\t\t\t| nickname          =\n\t\t\t\t\t| mascot            =\n\t\t\t\t\t| affiliations      =\n\t\t\t\t\t| website           = {{URL | http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/ }}\n\t\t\t\t\t| footnotes         =\n\t\t\t\t\t| image_name        =  IIT Ropar Official Logo.jpg\n\t\t\t\t\t}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe '''Indian Institute of Technology Ropar''' ('''IIT Ropar''') or '''IIT-RPR''', is an engineering and technology higher education institute located in [[Rupnagar]], [[Punjab, India|Punjab]], India. It is one of the eight newer [[Indian Institutes of Technology]] (IITs)<ref>{{cite web|title=IIT Ropar is now independent of IIT Delhi's mentoring and administration|url=http://economictimes.indiatimes.com/industry/services/education/iit-ropar-is-now-independent-of-iit-delhis-mentoring-and-administration/articleshow/48217835.cms}}</ref> established by the  [[Ministry of Human Resource Development (India)|Ministry of Human Resource Development]] MHRD, Government of India under The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Act, 2011.<ref name=AmendmentAct>{{cite web|url=http://www.prsindia.org/uploads/media/Institute%20of%20Technology%20Bill%202010.pdf|format=PDF|title=The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Bill, 2010| date = 23 August 2010}}</ref> The Act was passed in the [[Lok Sabha]] on 24 March 2011<ref>{{cite news |url= http://www.deccanherald.com/content/148456/ls-passes-bill-provide-iit.html |title=LS passes bill to provide IIT status to 8 institutes, BHU  |newspaper=Deccan Herald |date=24 March 2011 |accessdate=9 May 2011 | location = New Delhi}}</ref> and by the [[Rajya Sabha]] on 30 April 2012.<ref>{{cite news |url= http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/tech/careers/education/Parliament-passes-IIT-bill/articleshow/12937917.cms |title=Parliament passes IIT bill |newspaper=The Times of India |date=30 April 2012 |accessdate=30 April 2012}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==History==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar was established by MHRD in 2008. The classes for academic session 2008\u20132009 were held at [[IIT Delhi]]. The Institute started functioning from its transit campus in Rupnagar in August 2009.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://twocircles.net/2009aug07/iit_punjab_start_working_its_new_campus_aug_20.html |title=IIT Punjab to start working from its new campus Aug 20 |author = IANS/Indo-Asian News Service | publisher=TwoCircles.net |date=7 August 2009 | location = New Delhi |accessdate=2013-02-06}}</ref><ref>{{cite news| url=http://articles.timesofindia.indiatimes.com/2009-07-21/india/28211741_1_transit-campus-ropar-iit-delhi | work=The Times of India | title=Big milestone: IIT-Punjab classes from August 20 | date=21 July 2009}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus and location==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar is located at [[Rupnagar]] (formerly known as Ropar) town of the [[Rupnagar district|district Rupnagar]]. Rupnagar was founded in the 11th century and named after Rup Sen son of Raja Rokeshar. Recent excavations and explorations conducted at Rupnagar indicate that the first settlements here were the [[Indus Valley Civilization|Harappans]], who reached the upper [[Satluj]] towards the close of third millennium B.C. The district has rich historical and religious significance.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tRupnagar town is the headquarters of district Rupnagar and is located 42&nbsp;km. from [[Chandigarh]], the state capital. It is connected by road on [[Indian National Highways|National Highway]] [[NH-21]]. The [[Delhi]]-[[Ambala]]-[[Una, Himachal Pradesh|Una]] railway line passes through Rupnagar and provides rail connectivity. The nearest airport is at Chandigarh at a distance of about 60&nbsp;km. The [[Satluj]] river passes close to Rupnagar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe climate is characterised by its general dryness, except during the south-west monsoon season, a hot summer and a cold winter. The winter is from mid-November to February, summer from March to June and the monsoon from late June to mid-September. The average annual rainfall in the district is about 776&nbsp;mm with about 78% in the period of June to September.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Permanent campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe location for permanent campus of IIT Ropar is Birla Seed Farms, Rupnagar. The Government of Punjab has approved about {{convert|525|acre|km2}} land for the permanent campus in Rupnagar. Foundation stone for the permanent campus of IIT Ropar was laid down on 24 February 2009 by former Union HRD Minister [[Arjun Singh|Mr. Arjun Singh]]. The contract is given to CPWD and a Bangkok-based construction company is assigned the task of finishing the first phase. The college will be operational in the permanent campus from year 2018. \n\t\t\t\t\t[[File:IIT Ropar - Main Building of the Transit Campus.JPG|thumbnail|IIT Ropar transit campus]]\n\t\t\t\t\t<!-- [[File:IIT ROPAR.jpg|thumb|right|Temporary campus]] -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Temporary campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe temporary campus of IIT Ropar is former Women's Polytechnic, Rupnagar. The academic and administration buildings of the Women's Polytechnic were completely renovated to accommodate all the requirements of the Institute . It has all the basic infrastructure to run Academic programmes specially designed by IIT Delhi. The transit campus is equipped with state of art lecture halls along with well-maintained playgrounds to nurture the bright minds and enhance their overall development. Special emphasis has been laid to set up advanced laboratories to help students gain practical insight of the courses that are a part of their curriculum. The current temporary campus is a brief 1&nbsp;km walk from Rupnagar railway station.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t== Rankings ==\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Infobox India university ranking\n\t\t\t\t\t|type=University\n\n\t\t\t\t\t| NIRF_E_2017 = 21\n\t\t\t\t\t| NIRF_O_2017 = 32\n\t\t\t\t\t| IT_E_2017 = 25\n\t\t\t\t\t}}\n\t\t\t\t\tAmong engineering colleges, IIT Ropar ranked 25 by ''[[India Today]]'' in 2017<ref name=Rankings_IT_E_2017/> and 21 by the ''[[National Institutional Ranking Framework]]'' in 2017<ref name=Rankings_NIRF_E_2017/> and 32 overall.<ref name=Rankings_NIRF_O_2017/>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Departments==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute flagged its beginning with the following 10 departments including 4 engineering and 6 science departments, all of which offer PhD programme.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academics==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute offers undergraduate programmes awarding [[Bachelor of Technology]] in various engineering areas. Admission to these programmes is through [[JEE Advanced]].<ref>{{cite web|title=JEE Advanced 2017: Registration Ends; Know Details Here|url=https://www.ndtv.com/education/jee-advanced-2017-registration-ends-tomorrow-know-details-here-1688218|website=NDTV.com|accessdate=19 December 2017}}</ref> The institute also offers postgraduate degrees awarding M.Tech. and M.Sc. (Research) in various engineering fields, as well as M.Sc. in basic sciences.<ref>{{cite web|title=Admissions {{!}} Indian Institute of Technology Ropar|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/admissions|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|accessdate=19 December 2017}}</ref> Ph.D. courses in various fields are also offered.<ref>{{Cite web| url = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20120114175809/http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml | archivedate = 14 January 2012 | publisher = Indian Institute of Technology Ropar | title = PhD Admissions | date = January 2012 | accessdate = 6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus life/Infrastructure==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Hostel Facilities===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Institute campus houses five hostels: four for boys (Mercury Wings A, B & C, Jupiter and Neptune Houses) and one for girls (Venus House). The hostels are well equipped for comfortable lodging and boarding of approximately 550 students. All hostels are provided with water coolers and RO water filter systems. Each hostel has a common room that provides facilities for indoor recreation and games. The hostel complex also includes two laundry centers. High speed internet is available via wireless internet (spread in the complete campus area) and LAN connections provided by BSNL India.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe day-to-day management of hostels is taken care of by a committee consisting of student representatives, faculty members (as Wardens) and administrative staff (caretakers, office-heads).\n\t\t\t\t\tInstitute has its own independent post office opened for the staff and students of the institute. SBI (State Bank of India) has a well operational branch inside the campus premises.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Medical Facility===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute has allocated a separate building, which adjoins the hostel complex, for its medical facility. A doctor and a nurse have been appointed to attend to medical emergencies of the campus residents. There are both allopathic as well as homeopathic doctors available. In addition, the institute relies upon a few super-speciality hospitals in the city of Ropar for providing medical care to its members.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t[[File:Iit rpr.jpg|right|thumb|Football field at IIT Ropar]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Sports Facilities===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe students of the institute, apart from showing excellent academic progress, are keen to pursue their interests in sports and games. To nurture these interests, the institute provides several facilities. At present, the institute has a cricket field, three tennis courts, a football field, a gymnasium, a basketball court, two volleyball court and also a number of facilities for several athletics.\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute also encourages its students to participate in the inter-IIT competition which is held every year in December at different IIT campuses across India and other competitions.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Students Activity Center (SAC) has a well equipped gymnasium and rooms for different activity clubs such as the Music Club, Dance Club and the Fine Arts Club.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Central Library===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Central Library functions as the primary information resource and repository for all teaching and research activities at the institute. Apart from textbooks and recommended reading material prescribed for each course offered at the institute, the library houses a growing collection of research monographs, reports, multi-volume reference works, dictionaries, encyclopaedias, handbooks, and so on. In addition, the library also facilitates access to a number of journals through its participation in consortia such as INDEST-AICTE. At present, users can consult more than 4000 books (available on shelves) and hundreds of journals (through electronic subscription).<ref>{{cite web| url = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/centrallibrary.shtml | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20120504024741/http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/centrallibrary.shtml | archivedate = 4 May 2012 | title = Central Library | publisher = Indian Institute of Technology Ropar | accessdate = 6 February 2013 }}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Security===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute has ensured that its campus and residents are safe and secure. To accomplish this, a security agency has been entrusted with the task of providing security to its personnel and resources.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe beautiful campus has a peaceful environment.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://picasaweb.google.com/117707137521513270028 |publisher = Picasa Web Albums | title = IIT Ropar's Gallery (7 Albums) |date=8 May 2010 |accessdate=6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Extra Curricular Activities==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Societies & Clubs===\n\t\t\t\t\tThere are various societies being run by the student body at the institute to promote extra currulicular and co-curricular activities. These clubs ensure participation from the students in different institute level activities & competitions, and prepare them for inter-college competitions. The Fine Arts Club, The Music Society, The Dance Club, LitSoc- The Literary Society, The Chess Club, The Athletics Club, The Creative Writing Club, Science and Technology Club, etc. are managed by the respective student representatives and a secretary.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Zeitgeist===\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Zeitgeist (festival)|Zeitgeist]] is the annual cultural festival of Indian Institute of Technology Ropar and is held annually as a three-day festival in late Feb - early March. It was conceived in September 2010.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Advitiya===\n\t\t\t\t\tAdvitiya is the upcoming annual technical festival of Indian Institute of Technology Ropar to be held as a three-day festival in late March. Its maiden edition will be held from 22 March 2017 to 24 March 2017.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Music Society===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Music Society provides performance opportunities and brings live music to events during the academic year. Anyone who has an interest in playing an instrument, singing or appreciating music is welcome to join. In the Student Activity Center, is a music room with various instruments including a complete drum set, acoustic and electric guitars, and a keyboard. All details regarding this society can be found at http://iitrprmusicsociety.webs.com/\n\n\t\t\t\t\t=== Inter Batch Cultural Championship ===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Inter Batch Cultural Championship or IBCC is the inter batch cultural competition of IIT Ropar and was inaugurated in 2014 to instil competitiveness amongst the students. Dance, music, and art are included in the list of events.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Events held===\n\t\t\t\t\t*Saaz \u2013 Solo singing competition\n\t\t\t\t\t*Sur \u2013 Duet singing competition\n\t\t\t\t\t*Rashmi - Kavi Sammelan \n\t\t\t\t\t*Torque \u2013 Rock band competition (Part of [[Zeitgeist (festival)|Zeitgeist]])\n\t\t\t\t\t*Symphony \u2013 Western instrumental competition (Part of [[Zeitgeist (festival)|Zeitgeist]])\n\t\t\t\t\t*Raag \u2013 Indian instrumental competition (Part of [[Zeitgeist (festival)|Zeitgeist]])\n\t\t\t\t\t*[[Zeitgeist (festival)|Zeitgeist]] - cultural festival\n\t\t\t\t\t*Samagam - weekend cultural activities\n\t\t\t\t\t*Conclave - English debate\n\t\t\t\t\t*Viruddh - Hindi debate .\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Alumni association==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe IIT Ropar Alumni Association was founded on 1 February 2013. The association aims to encourage the alumni to take abiding interest in the progress and development of the institute. Since its establishment, the association has grown from strength to strength, regularly undertaking several initiatives to promote and foster mutually beneficial interaction between the alumni and the alma mater.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://alumni.iitrpr.ac.in |title=IIT Ropar Alumni Association}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==See also==\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[List of universities in India]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[Indian
