It is one of the eight newer [[Indian Institutes of Technology]] (IITs)<ref>{{cite web|title=IIT Ropar is now independent of IIT Delhi's mentoring and administration|url=http://economictimes.indiatimes.com/industry/services/education/iit-ropar-is-now-independent-of-iit-delhis-mentoring-and-administration/articleshow/48217835.cms}}</ref> established by the  [[Ministry of Human Resource Development (India)|Ministry of Human Resource Development]] (MHRD), [[Government of India]] under [[The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Act, 2011]].<ref name=AmendmentAct>{{cite web|url=http://www.prsindia.org/uploads/media/Institute%20of%20Technology%20Bill%202010.pdf|format=PDF|title=The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Bill, 2010| date = 23 August 2010}}</ref> The Act was passed in the [[Lok Sabha]] on 24 March 2011<ref>{{cite news |url= http://www.deccanherald.com/content/148456/ls-passes-bill-provide-iit.html |title=LS passes bill to provide IIT status to 8 institutes, BHU  |newspaper=Deccan Herald |date=24 March 2011 |accessdate=9 May 2011 | location = New Delhi}}</ref> and by the [[Rajya Sabha]] on 30 April 2012.<ref>{{cite news |url= http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/tech/careers/education/Parliament-passes-IIT-bill/articleshow/12937917.cms |title=Parliament passes IIT bill |newspaper=The Times of India |date=30 April 2012 |accessdate=30 April 2012}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==History==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar was established by MHRD in 2008. The classes for academic session 2008\u20132009 were held at [[IIT Delhi]]. The Institute started functioning from its transit campus in Rupnagar in August 2009.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://twocircles.net/2009aug07/iit_punjab_start_working_its_new_campus_aug_20.html |title=IIT Punjab to start working from its new campus Aug 20 |author = IANS/Indo-Asian News Service | publisher=TwoCircles.net |date=7 August 2009 | location = New Delhi |accessdate=2013-02-06}}</ref><ref>{{cite news| url=http://articles.timesofindia.indiatimes.com/2009-07-21/india/28211741_1_transit-campus-ropar-iit-delhi | work=The Times of India | title=Big milestone: IIT-Punjab classes from August 20 | date=21 July 2009}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus and location==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar is located at [[Rupnagar]] (formerly known as Ropar) at the [[Rupnagar district]], 42&nbsp;km. from [[Chandigarh]], the state capital. It is connected by road on [[Indian National Highways|National Highway]] [[NH-21]]. The [[Delhi]]-[[Ambala]]-[[Una, Himachal Pradesh|Una]] railway line passes through Rupnagar and provides rail connectivity. The nearest airport is at Chandigarh at a distance of about 60&nbsp;km. The [[Satluj]] river passes close to Rupnagar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Permanent campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe location for permanent campus of IIT Ropar is Birla Seed Farms, Rupnagar. The Government of Punjab has approved about {{convert|525|acre|km2}} land for the permanent campus in Rupnagar. Foundation stone for the permanent campus of IIT Ropar was laid down on 24 February 2009 by former Union HRD Minister [[Arjun Singh]]. The contract is given to CPWD and a Bangkok-based construction company is assigned the task of finishing the first phase.<ref>{{Cite web|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/Permanent%20Campus/|title=Permanent Campus \u2013 Indian Institute of Technology Ropar|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|language=en-GB|access-date=2017-12-20}}</ref> \n\t\t\t\t\t[[File:IIT Ropar - Main Building of the Transit Campus.JPG|thumbnail|IIT Ropar transit campus]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Temporary campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe temporary campus of IIT Ropar is former Women's Polytechnic, Rupnagar. The academic and administration buildings of the Women's Polytechnic, Ropar were completely renovated to accommodate all the requirements of the Institute . It has all the basic infrastructure to run Academic programmes specially designed by IIT Delhi. Lecture halls, advanced laboratories and playgrounds are present. The current temporary campus is a brief 1&nbsp;km walk from Rupnagar railway station.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t== Rankings ==\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Infobox India university ranking\n\t\t\t\t\t|type=University\n\t\t\t\t\t| NIRF_E_2018 = 22\n\t\t\t\t\t| IT_E_2017 = 25\n\t\t\t\t\t}}\n\t\t\t\t\tAmong engineering colleges, IIT Ropar ranked 25 by ''[[India Today]]'' in 2017<ref name=Rankings_IT_E_2017/> and 21 by the [[National Institutional Ranking Framework]] (NIRF) in 2018.<ref name=Rankings_NIRF_E_2018/>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Departments and Centres==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute currently has 9 departments and 2 multi-disciplinary centers. The departments are:\n\t\t\t\t\t* Chemical Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Chemistry\n\t\t\t\t\t* Civil Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Computer Science and Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Electrical Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Humanities and Social Sciences\n\t\t\t\t\t* Mathematics\n\t\t\t\t\t* Mechanical Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Physics\n\t\t\t\t\tThe following are the multi-disciplinary centers in IIT Ropar:\n\t\t\t\t\t* Center for Biomedical Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Center for Materials and Energy Engineering\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academics==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute offers undergraduate programmes awarding [[Bachelor of Technology]] in various engineering areas. Admission to these programmes is through [[JEE Advanced]].<ref>{{cite web|title=JEE Advanced 2017: Registration Ends; Know Details Here|url=https://www.ndtv.com/education/jee-advanced-2017-registration-ends-tomorrow-know-details-here-1688218|website=NDTV.com|accessdate=19 December 2017}}</ref> The institute also offers postgraduate degrees awarding M.Tech. and M.Sc. (Research) in various engineering fields, as well as M.Sc. in basic sciences.<ref>{{cite web|title=Admissions {{!}} Indian Institute of Technology Ropar|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/admissions|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|accessdate=19 December 2017}}</ref> Ph.D. courses in various fields are also offered.<ref>{{Cite web| url = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20120114175809/http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml | archivedate = 14 January 2012 | publisher = Indian Institute of Technology Ropar | title = PhD Admissions | date = January 2012 | accessdate = 6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus infrastructure==\n\t\t\t\t\t[[File:Iit rpr.jpg|right|thumb|Football field at IIT Ropar]]\n\t\t\t\t\tThe temporary campus houses four hostels: three for boys (Mercury Wings A, B & C, Jupiter and Neptune Houses) and one for girls (Venus House). The day-to-day management of hostels is taken care of by a committee consisting of student representatives, faculty members (as Wardens) and administrative staff (caretakers, office-heads). The institute has an independent post office and a branch of [[State Bank of India]] (SBI). There is also a central library in the campus, offering about 4,000 books.<ref>{{cite web| url = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/centrallibrary.shtml | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20120504024741/http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/centrallibrary.shtml | archivedate = 4 May 2012 | title = Central Library | publisher = Indian Institute of Technology Ropar | accessdate = 6 February 2013 }}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\tSport facilities include a cricket field, three tennis courts, a football field, a gymnasium, a basketball court, two volleyball court and also a number of facilities for several athletics. The Students Activity Center (SAC) has a gymnasium and rooms for different activity clubs.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Extra curricular activities==\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Zeitgeist (festival)|Zeitgeist]] is the annual cultural festival of Indian Institute of Technology Ropar and is held annually as a three-day festival in late Feb - early March. It was conceived in September 2010. Advitiya, with its maiden edition in 2017, is the annual technical festival, which is held for three days in March. An annual sports festival, Aarohan is also held annually during February. It is currently in its second edition. These college fests are managed financially and conducted entirely by the students. Also organized by the students and the faculty is an annual [[Indian classical music]] and [[Dance in India|dance]] event [[SPIC MACAY]].\n\n\t\t\t\t\tEvents such as Inter Batch Cultural Championship (IBCC) and Inter Year Sports Championship are the intra-college events that are organized annually for the students of the institute.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe management of student activities is done by many boards functioning under the Student Affairs Department. These boards have elected student representatives known as General Secretaries, and an overall elected President of the Student Council. They have various societies and clubs to promote extra curricular and co-curricular activities.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Alumni Association==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe IIT Ropar Alumni Association was founded on 1 February 2013. The association aims to encourage the alumni to take abiding interest in the progress and development of the institute. Since its establishment, the association has grown from strength to strength, regularly undertaking several initiatives to promote and foster mutually beneficial interaction between the alumni and the alma mater.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://alumni.iitrpr.ac.in |title=IIT Ropar Alumni Association}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==See also==\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[List of universities in India]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[Indian Institutes of Technology]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[Education in India]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==References==\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Reflist}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==External links==\n\t\t\t\t\t* {{official|http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Indian Institute Of Technology}}\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Portal bar|Education in India}}\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Authority control}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t{{DEFAULTSORT:Indian Institute Of Technology Punjab}}\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Indian Institutes of Technology|Ropar]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Educational institutions established in 2008]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Rupnagar]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Engineering colleges in Punjab, India]]\n\t\t\t\t"}, {"text": "6 -2 2013}}`\t\t{{Infobox 1215 "}, {"text": "`\t\t{{refimprove|date=April -1 2018}}`\t\t{{Use 1221 "}, {"text": "544 -1 8 Institute.``\t\t== -38 632 "}, {"text": "108 -1 Yellow<br/>{{color 321 -1 Rupnagar.``\t\t===Temporary -80 campus===`\t\t[[File:IIT 10 -2 campus]]`\t\tThe 29 -1 Institute.``\t\tThe -199 153 -1 clubs.``\t\t===Permanent campus===`\t\tThe location for permanent campus of IIT Ropar is Birla Seed Farms, Rupnagar. Indian Institute of Technology Ropar logo.png\n\t\t\t\t\t}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe '''Indian Institute of Technology Ropar''' ('''IIT Ropar''') or '''IIT-RPR''', is an engineering, science and technology higher education institute located in [[Rupnagar]], [[Punjab, India|Punjab]], [[India]]. It is one of the eight newer [[Indian Institutes of Technology]] (IITs)<ref>{{cite web|title=IIT Ropar is now independent of IIT Delhi's mentoring and administration|url=http://economictimes.indiatimes.com/industry/services/education/iit-ropar-is-now-independent-of-iit-delhis-mentoring-and-administration/articleshow/48217835.cms}}</ref> established by the [[Ministry of Human Resource Development (India)|Ministry of Human Resource Development]] (MHRD), [[Government of India]] under [[The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Act, 2011]].<ref name=AmendmentAct>{{cite web|url=http://www.prsindia.org/uploads/media/Institute%20of%20Technology%20Bill%202010.pdf|format=PDF|title=The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Bill, 2010| date = 23 August 2010}}</ref> The Act was passed in the [[Lok Sabha]] on 24 March 2011<ref>{{cite news |url= http://www.deccanherald.com/content/148456/ls-passes-bill-provide-iit.html |title=LS passes bill to provide IIT status to 8 institutes, BHU  |newspaper=Deccan Herald |date=24 March 2011 |accessdate=9 May 2011 | location = New Delhi}}</ref> and by the [[Rajya Sabha]] on 30 April 2012.<ref>{{cite news |url= http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/tech/careers/education/Parliament-passes-IIT-bill/articleshow/12937917.cms |title=Parliament passes IIT bill |newspaper=The Times of India |date=30 April 2012 |accessdate=30 April 2012}}</ref>\n\t\t\t\t\tIt is regularly considered to be among the top 10 IITs.\n\t\t\t\t\t==History==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar was established by MHRD in 2008. The classes for academic session 2008\u20132009 were held at [[IIT Delhi]]. The Institute started functioning from its transit campus in Rupnagar in August 2009.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://twocircles.net/2009aug07/iit_punjab_start_working_its_new_campus_aug_20.html |title=IIT Punjab to start working from its new campus Aug 20 |author = IANS/Indo-Asian News Service | publisher=TwoCircles.net |date=7 August 2009 | location = New Delhi |accessdate=2013-02-06}}</ref><ref>{{cite news| url=http://articles.timesofindia.indiatimes.com/2009-07-21/india/28211741_1_transit-campus-ropar-iit-delhi | work=The Times of India | title=Big milestone: IIT-Punjab classes from August 20 | date=21 July 2009}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute currently operates out of three different campuses located in Rupnagar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Transit Campus I===\n\t\t\t\t\t[[File:IIT Ropar - Main Building of the Transit Campus.JPG|thumbnail|The main academic block of Transit Campus I]]\n\t\t\t\t\tThe transit campus I of IIT Ropar is former Women's Polytechnic, Rupnagar. The academic and administration buildings of the Women's Polytechnic, Ropar were renovated to accommodate all the requirements of the Institute.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThis campus houses four hostels: three for boys (Mercury, Jupiter and Neptune Houses) and one for girls (Venus House). The day-to-day management of hostels is taken care of by a committee consisting of student representatives, faculty members (as Wardens) and administrative staff (caretakers, office-heads).\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThis campus currently houses the central library of the institute. It also an independent post office and a branch of [[State Bank of India]].\n\n\t\t\t\t\tSports facilities include a cricket field, three tennis courts, a football field, a gymnasium, a basketball court, two volleyball court and also a number of facilities for several athletics. The Students Activity Center (SAC) has a gymnasium and rooms for different activity clubs.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t=== Transit Campus II ===\n\n\t\t\t\t\tOwing to the [[Ministry of Human Resource Development]]'s (HRD) order for increasing seats, the institute started functioning from an additional transit campus. This campus is being shared by and leased from [[National Institute of Electronics & Information Technology|NIELIT]] Ropar. It is located adjacent to the permanent campus. Along with the main academic area, the campus has three hostels and three faculty residences.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tTransportation to and from the campus is mainly done via the institute busses, that ply between the two transit campuses.[[File:Iit rpr.jpg|thumbnail|Football Ground inside Transit Campus I]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Permanent Campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute has also started to operate from its permanent campus from July 2018. Various phases of this campus are still under construction. The campus is being built on the land earlier known as Birla Seed Farms. It is located over an area of {{convert|525|acre|km2}}. Foundation stone for the permanent campus was laid on 24 February 2009 by Union [[Ministry of Human Resource Development|HRD]] Minister [[Arjun Singh]]. The contract is given to [[Central Public Works Department|CPWD]] and a Bangkok-based construction company is assigned the task of finishing the first phase.<ref>{{Cite web|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/Permanent%20Campus/|title=Permanent Campus \u2013 Indian Institute of Technology Ropar|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|language=en-GB|access-date=2017-12-20}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Computer Science Department has been shifted to this campus in July 2018. A part of the administration office was shifted on 17th June 2018.\n\t\t\t\t\tAs of June 2019 the administration is completely shifted to the permanent campus. Department of Electrical,Computer Science and Mechanical Engineering are also shifted to the permanent campus. \n\t\t\t\t\t==Departments and Centres==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute currently has 10 departments and 1 multi-disciplinary centre.<ref>{{Cite web|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/departments-centers|title=Departments & Centers {{!}} Indian Institute of Technology Ropar|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|access-date=2018-04-29}}</ref> The departments are:\n\t\t\t\t\t* Chemical Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Chemistry\n\t\t\t\t\t* Civil Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Computer Science and Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Electrical Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Metallurgical and Materials Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Humanities and Social Sciences\n\t\t\t\t\t* Mathematics\n\t\t\t\t\t* Mechanical Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Physics\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe Center for Biomedical Engineering is the multi-disciplinary centre.\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academics==\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Expand Section|date=April 2018}}\n\t\t\t\t\t=== Programmes ===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute offers undergraduate programmes awarding [[Bachelor of Technology]] in various engineering areas. Admission to these programmes is through [[JEE Advanced]].<ref>{{cite web|title=JEE Advanced 2017: Registration Ends; Know Details Here|url=https://www.ndtv.com/education/jee-advanced-2017-registration-ends-tomorrow-know-details-here-1688218|website=NDTV.com|accessdate=19 December 2017}}</ref> The institute also offers postgraduate degrees awarding M.Tech. and M.Sc. (Research) in various engineering fields, as well as M.Sc. in basic sciences.<ref>{{cite web|title=Admissions {{!}} Indian Institute of Technology Ropar|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/admissions|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|accessdate=19 December 2017}}</ref> Ph.D. courses in various fields are also offered.<ref>{{Cite web| url = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20120114175809/http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml | archivedate = 14 January 2012 | publisher = Indian Institute of Technology Ropar | title = PhD Admissions | date = January 2012 | accessdate = 6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t=== Rankings ===\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Infobox India university ranking\n\t\t\t\t\t| type=University\n\t\t\t\t\t| QS_BRICS_2019 = 107\n\t\t\t\t\t| QS_A_2019 = 219\n\t\t\t\t\t| QS_INDIA_2019 = 21\n\t\t\t\t\t| NIRF_E_2018 = 22\n\t\t\t\t\t| IT_E_G_2018 = 11\n\t\t\t\t\t}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\tAmong government engineering colleges, IIT Ropar has been ranked 11 by ''[[India Today]]''<ref name=Rankings_IT_E_G_2018/> and 22 by the [[National Institutional Ranking Framework]] (NIRF) in engineering colleges for 2018.<ref name=Rankings_NIRF_E_2018/> The institute has been featured in the ''[[QS World University Rankings]]'' for the first time in 2018, and was ranked 107 in [[BRICS]]<ref name=Rankings_QS_BRICS_2019/> and 219 in Asia.<ref name=Rankings_QS_A_2019/>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t=== Research ===\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Expand section|date=April 2018}}\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute stresses in inter-disciplinary research areas including Renewable and Clean Energy, Bio-imaging and Bio-instrumentation, and Agriculture and Rural Development.<ref>{{Cite web|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/our-interdisciplinary-thrust-areas|title=Our interdisciplinary thrust areas {{!}} Indian Institute of Technology Ropar|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|access-date=2018-04-29}}</ref> A Central Research Facility has been established encompassing equipment from various departments.<ref>{{Cite web|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/crf/|title=Central Research Facilities  \u2013 Indian Institute of Technology Ropar|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|language=en-US|access-date=2018-04-29}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\tIn the academic year 2017-18, the institute organized its first Research Conclave.<ref>{{Cite web|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/research_conclave/|title=Research Conclave IIT Ropar|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|access-date=2018-04-29}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news|url=https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/home/education/news/top-scholars-seek-to-prioritize-innovative-research-as-one-day-conclave-concluded-at-iit-ropar/articleshow/63877597.cms|title=Top scholars seek to prioritize innovative research as one-day conclave concluded at IIT Ropar - Times of India|work=The Times of India|access-date=2018-04-29}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Extra curricular activities==\n\t\t\t\t\tZeitgeist is the annual cultural festival of Indian Institute of Technology Ropar and is held annually as a three-day festival in late Feb - early March.<ref name=\":0\">{{Cite web|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/student-affairs/boca/|title=Board of Cultural Activities|last=Agarwal|first=Rohan|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|language=en|access-date=2018-04-29}}</ref> It was conceived in September 2010. Advitiya, with its maiden edition in 2017, is the annual technical festival, which is held for three days in March. An annual sports festival, Aarohan is also held annually during February. It is currently in its second edition.<ref name=\":1\">{{Cite web|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/student-affairs/bosa/|title=Board of Sports Activities|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|language=en|access-date=2018-04-29}}</ref> These college fests are managed financially and conducted entirely by the students. An annual [[Indian classical music]] and [[Dance in India|dance]] event [[SPIC MACAY]]<ref name=\":0\" /> is also organized by the students and the faculty.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tEvents such as Inter Batch Cultural Championship (IBCC) and Inter Year Sports Championship are the intra-college events that are organized annually for the students of the institute.<ref name=\":0\" /><ref name=\":1\" />\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe management of student activities is done by many boards functioning under the Student Affairs Department. These boards have elected student representatives known as General Secretaries, and an overall elected President of the Student Council. They have various societies and clubs to promote extra curricular and co-curricular activities.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Alumni Association==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe IIT Ropar Alumni Association was founded on 1 February 2013. The association aims to encourage the alumni to take abiding interest in the progress and development of the institute. Since its establishment, the association has grown from strength to strength, regularly undertaking several initiatives to promote and foster mutually beneficial interaction between the alumni and the alma mater.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://alumni.iitrpr.ac.in |title=IIT Ropar Alumni Association}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==See also==\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[List of universities in India]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[Indian Institutes of Technology]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[Education in India]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[:Category:Engineering colleges in Punjab, India|Engineering colleges in Punjab, India]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==References==\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Reflist}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==External links==\n\t\t\t\t\t* {{official|http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Indian Institute Of Technology}}\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Authority control}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t{{DEFAULTSORT:Indian Institute Of Technology Punjab}}\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Indian Institutes of Technology|Ropar]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Educational institutions established in 2008]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Rupnagar]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Engineering colleges in Punjab, India]]\n\t\t\t\t"}, {"text": "301 -1 '23' -1 IITs.``\t\t==History==`\t\tIIT 1117 "}, {"text": "762 -1 2019, 1 -1 Administration and -8 Departments 1 -1 Electrical, Computer 4 -2 has been completely 639 "}, {"text": "757 -1 '17' 658 "}, {"text": "91 -1 {{Coord|30.9704|76.4691|type:edu|display=inline,title}}`\t\t| 1324 "}, {"text": "214 -1 2011]]<ref 13 -18 1 -5 expand the reach and enhance the quality of technical education in the country.This -1 institute is committed to providing state^of^the^art technical education in a variety of fields -14 1 -4 also for facilitating transmission of knowledge in keeping with latest developments in pedagogy. \n\t\t\t\t\t| former_names = \n\t\t\t\t\t| free_label = \n\t\t\t\t\t| free = \n\t\t\t\t\t| athletics = \n\t\t\t\t\t| colours = {{color box|yellow}} Yellow<br/>{{color box|green}} Green\n\t\t\t\t\t| Indian Institute of Technology Ropar logo.png\n\t\t\t\t\t}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe '''Indian Institute of Technology Ropar''' ('''IIT Ropar''') or '''IIT-RPR''', is an engineering, science and technology higher education institute located in [[Rupnagar]], [[Punjab, India|Punjab]], [[India]]. It is one of the eight newer [[Indian Institutes of Technology]] (IITs)<ref>{{cite web|title=IIT Ropar is now independent of IIT Delhi's mentoring and administration|url=http://economictimes.indiatimes.com/industry/services/education/iit-ropar-is-now-independent-of-iit-delhis-mentoring-and-administration/articleshow/48217835.cms}}</ref> established by the [[Ministry of Human Resource Development (India)|Ministry of Human Resource Development]] (MHRD), [[Government of India]] under [[The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Act, 2011]]<ref name=AmendmentAct>{{cite web|url=http://www.prsindia.org/uploads/media/Institute%20of%20Technology%20Bill%202010.pdf|title=The Institutes of Technology (Amendment) Bill, 2010| date = 23 August 2010}}</ref> to expand the reach and enhance the quality of technical education in the country.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==History==\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar was established by MHRD in 2008. The classes for academic session 2008\u20132009 were held at [[IIT Delhi]]. The Institute started functioning from its transit campus in Rupnagar in August 2009.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://twocircles.net/2009aug07/iit_punjab_start_working_its_new_campus_aug_20.html |title=IIT Punjab to start working from its new campus Aug 20 |author = IANS/Indo-Asian News Service | publisher=TwoCircles.net |date=7 August 2009 | location = New Delhi |accessdate=2013-02-06}}</ref><ref>{{cite news| url=http://articles.timesofindia.indiatimes.com/2009-07-21/india/28211741_1_transit-campus-ropar-iit-delhi | work=The Times of India | title=Big milestone: IIT-Punjab classes from August 20 | date=21 July 2009}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Campus==\n\t\t\t\t\t===Permanent Campus===\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar has completely shifted to its permanent campus since June 2019.<ref>{{cite web | title=IIT-Ropar shifts to permanent campus | website=The Tribune | date=2019-06-08 | url=https://www.tribuneindia.com/news/chandigarh/iit-ropar-shifts-to-permanent-campus/784699.html | access-date=2019-08-08}}</ref> Campus architecture is inspired by [[Indus Valley Civilisation]] with four 41 feet high stone carved<ref>{{Cite web|url=https://www.outlookindia.com/newsscroll/iit-ropar-gets-tallest-contemporary-stonecarved-pillars/1676903|title=IIT Ropar gets tallest contemporary stone-carved pillars|website=Outlook India|access-date=2020-01-22}}</ref> pillars at the entrance.<ref>{{Cite web|url=https://indianexpress.com/article/express-sunday-eye/written-in-stone-the-indian-institute-of-technology-ropar-harappan-6175069/|title=How IIT Ropar is honouring the storied past of its location with a modern tribute|date=2019-12-22|website=The Indian Express|language=en-US|access-date=2020-01-22}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web|url=https://www.indiawest.com/news/global_indian/iit-ropar-installs-unique-indus-valley-inspired-pillars/article_db850b68-2e57-11ea-8a3b-2fbd680283ca.html|title=IIT Ropar Installs Unique Indus Valley Inspired Pillars|last=Reporter|first=India-West Staff|website=India West|language=en|access-date=2020-01-22}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web|url=https://www.hindustantimes.com/chandigarh/pillars-depicting-ancient-history-come-up-at-iit-ropar/story-FTxQWVOidOkxA2bJIudtwO.html|title=Pillars depicting ancient history erected at IIT Ropar|date=2019-12-03|website=Hindustan Times|language=en|access-date=2020-01-22}}</ref> The institute started to operate from its permanent campus from July 2018. Some phases of this campus were still under construction. The campus was being built on the land earlier known as Birla Seed Farms. It is located over an area of {{convert|525|acre|km2}}. Foundation stone for the permanent campus was laid on 24 February 2009 by Union [[Ministry of Human Resource Development|HRD]] Minister [[Arjun Singh (politician, born 1930)|Arjun Singh]]. The contract was given to [[Central Public Works Department|CPWD]] and a Bangkok-based construction company was assigned the task of finishing the first phase.<ref>{{Cite web|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/Permanent%20Campus/|title=Permanent Campus \u2013 Indian Institute of Technology Ropar|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|language=en-GB|access-date=2017-12-20}}</ref> The Computer Science Department has been shifted to this campus in July 2018. A part of the administration office was shifted on 17 June 2018. In June 2019, the Administration and Departments of Electrical, Computer Science and Mechanical Engineering completely shifted to the permanent campus.\n \n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute in the past operated in two different transit campuses located in Rupnagar.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t===Transit Campus I===\n\t\t\t\t\t[[File:IIT Ropar - Main Building of the Transit Campus.JPG|thumbnail|The main academic block of Transit Campus I]]\n\t\t\t\t\tThe transit campus I of IIT Ropar is former Women's Polytechnic, Rupnagar. The academic and administration buildings of the Women's Polytechnic, Ropar were renovated to accommodate all the requirements of the Institute.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThis campus houses four hostels: three for boys (Mercury, Jupiter and Neptune Houses) and one for girls (Venus House). The day-to-day management of hostels is taken care of by a committee consisting of student representatives, faculty members (as Wardens) and administrative staff (caretakers, office-heads).\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThis campus currently houses the central library of the institute. It also an independent post office and a branch of [[State Bank of India]].\n\n\t\t\t\t\tSports facilities include a cricket field, three tennis courts, a football field, a gymnasium, a basketball court, two volleyball court and also a number of facilities for several athletics. The Students Activity Center (SAC) has a gymnasium and rooms for different activity clubs.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t=== Transit Campus II ===\n\n\t\t\t\t\tOwing to the [[Ministry of Human Resource Development]]'s (HRD) order for increasing seats, the institute started functioning from an additional transit campus. This campus has been shared by and leased from [[National Institute of Electronics & Information Technology|NIELIT]] Ropar. It is located adjacent to the permanent campus. IIT Ropar does not use this campus anymore.[[File:Iit rpr.jpg|thumbnail|Football Ground inside Transit Campus I]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Departments and Centres==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute currently has 10 departments, 1 multi-disciplinary centre <ref>{{Cite web|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/departments-centers|title=Departments & Centers {{!}} Indian Institute of Technology Ropar|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|access-date=2018-04-29}}</ref> and 1 DST Technology Innovation Hub.<ref>{{cite web | title=Centre Grants Rs 110 Crore To Set Up Technology Hub At IIT Ropar | website=NDTV | date=2020-08-08 | url=https://www.ndtv.com/education/centre-grants-rs110-cr-for-setting-up-technology-hub-at-iit-ropar | access-date=2020-08-08}}</ref> The departments are:\n\t\t\t\t\t* Chemical Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Chemistry\n\t\t\t\t\t* Civil Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Computer Science and Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Mathematics and Computing\n\t\t\t\t\t* Electrical Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Metallurgical and Materials Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Humanities and Social Sciences\n\t\t\t\t\t* Mathematics\n\t\t\t\t\t* Mechanical Engineering\n\t\t\t\t\t* Center for Biomedical Engineering\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==DST Technology Innovation Hub==\n\t\t\t\t\tIn 2020, the Department of Science of Technology (DST) has established a Technology Innovation Hub (TIH) in the application domain of Agriculture & Water, named as Agriculture and Water Technology Development Hub (AWaDH),at IIT Ropar in the framework of National Mission on Interdisciplinary Cyber-Physical Systems (NM-ICPS) with a grant of 110 crore. <ref>{{cite web | title=Centre Grants Rs 110 Crore To Set Up Technology Hub At IIT Ropar | website=NDTV | date=2020-08-08 | url=https://www.ndtv.com/education/centre-grants-rs110-cr-for-setting-up-technology-hub-at-iit-ropar | access-date=2020-08-08}}</ref> The innovation hub is aimed to bring solutions for stubble management, water quality improvement, mapping of hazardous substances in water and soil, and their treatment using next generation cyber-physical systems.<ref>{{cite web | title=Centre grants Rs 110 crore for setting up technology hub at IIT Ropar | website=Business Standard | date=2020-08-08 | url=https://www.business-standard.com/article/education/centre-grants-rs-110-crore-for-setting-up-technology-hub-at-iit-ropar-120080801098_1.html | access-date=2020-08-08}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Academics==\n\n\t\t\t\t\t=== Programmes ===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute offers undergraduate programmes awarding [[Bachelor of Technology]] in various engineering areas. Admission to these programmes is through [[JEE Advanced]].<ref>{{cite web|title=JEE Advanced 2017: Registration Ends; Know Details Here|url=https://www.ndtv.com/education/jee-advanced-2017-registration-ends-tomorrow-know-details-here-1688218|website=NDTV.com|accessdate=19 December 2017}}</ref> The institute also offers postgraduate degrees awarding MTech and MSc (Research) in various engineering fields, as well as MSc in basic sciences.<ref>{{cite web|title=Admissions {{!}} Indian Institute of Technology Ropar|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/admissions|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|accessdate=19 December 2017}}</ref> PhD courses in various fields are also offered.<ref>{{Cite web| url = http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml | archiveurl = https://web.archive.org/web/20120114175809/http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/html/phdadmission.shtml | archivedate = 14 January 2012 | publisher = Indian Institute of Technology Ropar | title = PhD Admissions | date = January 2012 | accessdate = 6 February 2013}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t=== Rankings ===\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Infobox India university ranking\n\t\t\t\t\t| type=University\n\t\t\t\t\t| QS_BRICS_2019 = 107\n\t\t\t\t\t| QS_A_2020 = 205\n\t\t\t\t\t| THE_W_2020 = 301-350\n\t\t\t\t\t| QS_INDIA_2020 = 25\n\t\t\t\t\t| NIRF_E_2020 = 25\n\t\t\t\t\t| IT_E_2020 = 11\n\t\t\t\t\t}}\n\t\t\t\t\tIIT Ropar has ranked on 205th position in the QS Asia Ranking 2020,<ref name=\"Rankings_QS_A_2020\" /> ranked 107th among the universities in BRICS countries by the QS BRICS Ranking 2019.<ref name=\"Rankings_QS_BRICS_2019\" />\n\t\t\t\t\tThe ''[[Times Higher Education World University Rankings]]'' ranked it 301-350 globally in the 2020 ranking.<ref name=Rankings_THE_W_2020/>\n\t\t\t\t\tThe [[National Institutional Ranking Framework]] (NIRF) ranked it 25th among engineering colleges in 2020<ref name=Rankings_NIRF_E_2020 />\n\n\t\t\t\t\t=== Research ===\n\t\t\t\t\tThe institute stresses in inter-disciplinary research areas including Renewable and Clean Energy, [[Artificial intelligence]]<ref>{{cite web | title=Indo-Taiwan AI research centre opens at IIT-Ropar | website=The Tribune| date=2019-07-28 | url=https://www.tribuneindia.com/news/chandigarh/indo-taiwan-ai-research-centre-opens-at-iit-ropar/808894.html | access-date=2019-08-08}}</ref> (AI), Bio-imaging and Bio-instrumentation, and Agriculture and Rural Development.<ref>{{Cite web|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/our-interdisciplinary-thrust-areas|title=Our interdisciplinary thrust areas {{!}} Indian Institute of Technology Ropar|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|access-date=2018-04-29}}</ref> A Central Research Facility has been established encompassing equipment from various departments.<ref>{{Cite web|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/crf/|title=Central Research Facilities  \u2013 Indian Institute of Technology Ropar|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|language=en-US|access-date=2018-04-29}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\tIn the academic year 2017-18, the institute organized its first Research Conclave.<ref>{{Cite web|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/research_conclave/|title=Research Conclave IIT Ropar|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|access-date=2018-04-29}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news|url=https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/home/education/news/top-scholars-seek-to-prioritize-innovative-research-as-one-day-conclave-concluded-at-iit-ropar/articleshow/63877597.cms|title=Top scholars seek to prioritize innovative research as one-day conclave concluded at IIT Ropar - Times of India|work=The Times of India|access-date=2018-04-29}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Extra curricular activities==\n\t\t\t\t\tZeitgeist is the annual cultural festival of Indian Institute of Technology Ropar and is held annually as a three-day festival in October or November.<ref name=\":0\">{{Cite web|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/student-affairs/boca/|title=Board of Cultural Activities|last=Agarwal|first=Rohan|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|language=en|access-date=2018-04-29}}</ref> It was conceived in September 2010. Advitiya, with its maiden edition in 2017, is the annual technical festival, which is held for three days in February or March. An annual sports festival, Aarohan is also held annually during February. It is currently in its second edition.<ref name=\":1\">{{Cite web|url=http://www.iitrpr.ac.in/student-affairs/bosa/|title=Board of Sports Activities|website=www.iitrpr.ac.in|language=en|access-date=2018-04-29}}</ref> These college fests are managed financially and conducted entirely by the students. An annual [[Indian classical music]] and [[Dance in India|dance]] event [[SPIC MACAY]]<ref name=\":0\" /> is also organized by the students and the faculty.\n\n\t\t\t\t\tEvents such as Inter Batch Cultural Championship (IBCC) and Inter Year Sports Championship are the intra-college events that are organized annually for the students of the institute.<ref name=\":0\" /><ref name=\":1\" />\n\n\t\t\t\t\tThe management of student activities is done by many boards functioning under the Student Affairs Department. These boards have elected student representatives known as General Secretaries, and an overall elected President of the Student Council. They have various societies and clubs to promote extra curricular and co-curricular activities.\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==Alumni Association==\n\t\t\t\t\tThe IIT Ropar Alumni Association was founded on 1 February 2013.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://alumni.iitrpr.ac.in |title=IIT Ropar Alumni Association}}</ref>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==See also==\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[List of universities in India]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[Indian Institutes of Technology]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[Education in India]]\n\t\t\t\t\t* [[:Category:Engineering colleges in Punjab, India|Engineering colleges in Punjab, India]]\n\n\t\t\t\t\t==References==\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Reflist}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Indian Institutes of Technology}}\n\t\t\t\t\t{{Authority control}}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t{{DEFAULTSORT:Indian Institute of Technology Punjab}}\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Indian Institutes of Technology|Ropar]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Educational institutions established in 2008]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Rupnagar]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Engineering colleges in Punjab, India]]\n\t\t\t\t\t[[Category:Research institutes in Punjab, India]]\n\t\t\t\t"}, {"text": "937 -24 52 | access^date=2020^08^08}}</ref> <ref>{{cite web | title=Rs '110' Crore To Set Up Technology Hub At IIT Ropar| website=Hindustan Times | date=2020^08^08 | url=https://www.hindustantimes.com/education/centre^grants^rs110^cr^for^setting^up^technology^hub^at^iit^ropar/story^dKzifJBLxodVgfseQl8MJI.html 557 "}, {"text": "935 Rs. 633 "}, {"text": "917 -1 (AWaDH), at 12 -1 (NM^ICPS)<ref>{{cite web | title=National Mission on Interdisciplinary Cyber Physical Systems | website=Science and Engineering Research Board (SERB) | date=2020^08^08 | url=https://serbonline.in/ICPS/HomePage | access^date=2020^08^08}}</ref> 638 "}, {"text": "569 -1 institute, 2 -1 past, 8 -1 Rupnagar.`\t\t[[File:/Users/pps/Desktop/Images wiki/spiraliitropar.jpg|thumb|The Spiral ^ an artistic representation of the DNA structure.
